	 Srinivasamakhi Vedantadesika: Dasavidhahetunirupana (part of the Vaikhanasasutratatparyacintamani)
Based on (pp. 1-122) the of the Devanāgarī-ed. by R. Parthasarathi Bhattacarya:
Śrīvaikhānasagṛhyasūtra (= DHN[D]); 2 vols., Akulamannāḍu, 1967 (reprint Tirupati, 1997/98).

FURTHER NOTES BY THE CONTRIBUTOR:
Die in eckige Klammern gesetzten Angaben im Text sowie die Anmerkungen sind Ergänzungen von Ute Hüsken.
Die Angaben aus dem Inhaltsverzeichnis der Devanāgarī-Edition sind in eckigen Klammern als Zwischenüberschriften in den Text eingefügt.
Die Quellennachweise bei Zitaten stehen in eckigen Klammern am rechten Rand oder in den Anmerkungen - dort ohne eckige Klammern.
Abweichende Lesarten der älteren Telugu-Ausgabe des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa (Abk.: DHN[T]; s.u.) sowie der zitierten Texte sind gelegentlich in Anmerkungen notiert, jedoch nicht durchgängig.*{1}*
Wird im Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa durch kurze Zitate auf längere Textzusammenhänge Bezug genommen, sind diese - sofern verifiziert - an der ersten Stelle ihres Vorkommens vollständig in den Anmerkungen zitiert. An weiteren Stellen wird auf das erste Zitat verwiesen. Die Verse sind in der vorliegenden Textwiedergabe der Ausgabe folgend eingerückt, Daṇḍas im Prosa-Text durch Punkte und Kommata ersetzt.
Das Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa liegt in zwei Editionen vor,*{2}* die beide von dem Vaikhānasa-Gelehrten Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya besorgt wurden. Die erste Edition erschien 1931 in Telugu-Schrift und umfaßt als Grundtext nur das Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa.
Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa by Śrīnivāsa Dīkṣita [in Telugu-script], ed. as Śrīvaikhānasasūtratātparyacintāmaṇidhṛto Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇākhyo bhāgaḥ, with Sanskrit-commentary and explanations in Telugu by Rompicarla Bhattar Srinivasa Aiyangar, Igavaripalem, 1931 (Śrīvaikhānasagranthamālā, Anubandha 5).
Wenngleich dieser Telugu-Druck an vielen Stellen die vermutlich richtigere Lesart enthält und die darin gegebenen Zitate den zitierten Texten in der uns heute gedruckt vorliegenden Form häufig näherkommen, ist der Textwiedergabe in der vorliegenden Arbeit die 36 Jahre später erschienene Devanāgarī-Edition zugrunde gelegt, da der Telugu-Druck an vielen Stellen nicht mehr lesbar ist. Zudem ist die ältere Telugu-Edition des Textes weltweit nur in wenigen Bibliotheken vorhanden und wegen der Brüchigkeit des Papiers kaum zu benutzen. Selbst im vorbildlich restaurierten Exemplar der Niedersächsischen Staats-und Universitätsbibliothek Göttingen (Signatur A 2000 A 35512) sind etliche Passagen unleserlich. Der Edition von 1931 in Telugu-Schrift ist neben dem Text des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa auch der Sanskrit-Kommentar Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇavyākhyāna (Abk.: DHNV) und eine Telugu-Erläuterung des Herausgebers beigegeben. Zudem enthält das Werk noch einen Zitatindex von 13 Seiten, so daß das Buch insgesamt stattliche 748 Druckseiten umfaßt. Der Umfang des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇavyākhyāna übertrifft dabei den des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa selbst bei weitem. Im Vorwort dieser Ausgabe äußert der Herausgeber sich nicht zu den der Edition zugrunde liegenden Manuskripten.
In der zweiten Edition von 1967 gab Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya das Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa zusammen mit dem Tātparyacintāmaṇi in zwei Bänden in Devanāgarī-Schrift heraus. Der Text dieser Ausgabe umfaßt 122 Druckseiten. Im Vorwort gibt Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya zu den dabei benutzten Manuskripten lediglich an, daß sie ihm sämtlich von Vaikhānasa-Familien zur Verfügung gestellt worden seien, und daß alle Manuskripte hinsichtlich der Fehler und Auslassungen identisch seien ("Introduction", S. v). Es ist davon auszugehen, daß er für diese Edition mindestens drei Handschriften konsultierte, die ihm drei Personen aus Andhra Pradesh (Ākuḷamannāḍu, Tirupati, Nallūru) überließen ("Introduction", S. viii). Da Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya seine Telugu-Edition des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa von 1931 mit keinem Wort erwähnt, bleibt unklar, ob er ganz andere Manuskripte verwendete oder ob die textliche Basis beider Editionen identisch ist.
-----
!{1}! Besonderheiten des Telugu-Textes, die den Gepflogenheiten alter Telugu-Drucke entsprechen, sind nicht gesondert vermerkt (s. dazu Grünendahl, 2001, S. xviiff.). Auf abweichende Lesarten im Telugu-Druck weist die Abkürzung "DHN[T]" mit Seitenzahl, aber ohne Zeilenangabe hin. Diese Unterscheide zwischen Devanāgarī- und Telugu-Ausgabe sind allerdings hier noch nicht vollständig erfaßt
!{2}! In keiner der beiden Editionen sind Lesarten angegeben.

daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa

 [maṅgalācaraṇam]

[1.1] śrīmadvikhanasa mahāgurave namaḥ /
[1.2] śrī śrīnivāsa parabrahmaṇe namaḥ //

[1.3-4] śrī śrīnivāsamakhikṛte śrīvaikhānasagṛhyasūtratātparyacintāmaṇau daśavidhahetunirūpaṇam
[1.5] vaikhānasakulodbhūtaṃ veṅkaṭeśārcanāratam*{3}* /
[1.6] vedāntadeśikaṃ vande śrīnivāsāryadīkṣitam //

[1.7] śrīveṅkaṭeśam akhileśam anantam ādyaṃ kāruṇyavāridhim aśeṣasurais suvandyam /
[1.8] vande samastajagatāṃ sthitisṛṣṭihetuṃ mānyān gurūṃś ca śataśo*{4}* bhṛgukaśyapādīn //

[1.9] śrutismṛtinadīpūrṇaṃ śāstrakallolasaṅkulam /
[1.10] viṣṇubhaktyudakaṃ śuddhaṃ vande vaikhānasārṇavam* //{5}*

[1.11] yenānyakḷptasūtrāṇāṃ*{6}* netraṃ nistimirīkṛtam /
[1.12] sūtraṃ vaikhānasaṃ hy etat*{7}* caturvargaphalapradam //

[1.13] śrutismṛtītihāsādyaiḥ pratipāditavaibhavām /
[1.14] paramātmaparāṃ vande sūtropaniṣadaṃ parām //

 [vyākhyānakartṛgotranāmādi]

[1.15] śrīmatkauśikavaṃśyena*{8}* govindācāryasūnunā /
[1.16] śrīveṅkaṭeśapādābjasaparyāsu ratātmanā //

[1.17] śrutismṛtipurāṇādisiddhamārgānuvartinā /
[1.18] pūrvācāryaparikṣuṇṇasampradāyānuyāyinā //

[1.19] vedāntācāryavaryeṇa śrīnivāsāryayajvanā /
[1.20] vaikhānasasya sūtrasya vyākhyā samyak prakāśyate //

!{3}! dhn[t] 1: veṅkaṭeśārcanāvaram.      

[vikhānasasūtrasya tadanuyāyināṃ ca sarvotkṛṣṭatve daśavidhahetūnāṃ nirdeśaḥ]

[2.1-3] atha satyatvādisamastakalyāṇaguṇaviśiṣṭāt parabrahmaṇaḥ śrīmannārāyaṇād utpannena vikhanaśśabdavācyena caturmukhabrahmaṇā praṇītasya vaikhānasasūtrasya sarvasūtrottamatve tatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhātṝṇāṃ sarvotkṛṣṭatamatve ca daśavidhahetavo nirūpyante. [2.4] yathā: [2.5-9] akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtena vikhanasā praṇītatvāt.*{9}* sarvasūtrāṇām āditvāt.*{10}* sarvakarmasu śrutimārgānusāritvāt.*{11}* samantrakasarvakriyāpratipādakatvāt.*{12}* niṣekasaṃskārādimatvāt.*{13}* aṣṭādaśaśārīrasaṃskārapratipādakatvāt.*{14}* sāṅgakriyākalāpavattvāt.*{15}* manvādyaiḥ svīkṛtatvāt.*{16}* akhilajagadekakāraṇabhūtaśrīmannārāyaṇaikaparatvāt.*{17}* etatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhānavatām eva bhagavatpriyatamatvopapatteś ca.*{18}* iti. [2.10-12] ebhir hetubhir asya sūtrasya sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ etatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhānād eva vaikhānasānāṃ sarvebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamatvāñ ca śrutismṛtipurāṇādimukhena pratipādyate. tatrādau akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtena vikhanasā praṇītatvād iti hetur nirūpyate. [2.13] vikhanaśśabdārthanirṇayaḥ

 [nārāyaṇasya vikhano vaikhānasādiśabdavācyatvam]

[2.14] vikhanā nāma kaścid ṛṣiḥ, uta nārāyaṇaḥ? nārāyaṇa eva kevalaṃ. [2.15-16] munimātrasya vaikhānasaśabdavācyatvena pratipādanābhāvāt. paramātmano nārāyaṇasya vikhano vaikhānasādiśabdavācyatvaṃ śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣv avagamyate. yathā: [2.17] khilaśrutau: "dhenur vahāṇām aditis surāṇāṃ brahmā ṛbhūṇāṃ vikhanā munīnām".

[2.18-19] iti śruyate. ayam arthaḥ. vahānāṃ ataḍudādīnāṃ dhenuḥ utpattikāraṇam. surāṇāṃ indrādīnām aditiḥ. ṛbhūṇāṃ:
[2.20] "sādhyā viśve ca vasavo maruto ṛbhavas tathā /
[2.21] tathaivāṅgiraso rudrā ādityāś ca tathaiva ca /
[2.22] ete devagaṇāś cāṣṭau manvantaragaṇeśvarāḥ //"
[2.23] iti bhṛgūktānāṃ sādhyādīnāṃ brahmā. munīnāṃ muniśabdavācyānāṃ vikhanāḥ.[2.24] brahmaṇo muniśabdavācyatvaṃ bhārate cāvagamyate[2.25] "niśāṃ suptvātha bhagavān kṣapānte pratyabuddhyata* /{19}* [mbh 13, app. 3.265][3.1] paścād buddhvā sasarjāpaḥ tāsu vīryam avāsṛjat* //{20}* [mbh 13, app. 3.266][3.2] tad aṇḍam abhavad dhaimaṃ sahasrāṃśusamaprabham / [mbh 13, app. 3.267][3.3] ahaṅkṛtyā*{21}* tatas tasmin sasarja prabhur īśvaraḥ / [mbh 13, app. 3.268][3.4] hiraṇyagarbhaṃ viśvātmā brahmāṇaṃ jalajaṃ*{22}* munim //" iti [mbh 13, app. 3.269][3.5] aṇḍabahutvābhiprāyeṇa munīnām iti bahuvacanam. yathā[3.6] "aṇḍānān tu sahasrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇy ayutāni ca /[3.7] īdṛśānām anantānāṃ koṭikoṭiśatāni ce//"ti smaraṇāt.[3.8] niśā cātra pralayaḥ, sā etāvatīti kutrāvagamyata iti cet.[3.9] mahābhārate: "caturyugasahasrāṇi caturyugaśatāni ca*{23}* / [mbh 13, app. 3.261][3.10] prāhuḥ kalpasahasran tu*{24}* brāhmaṇās tattvadarśinaḥ / [mbh 13, app. 3.262][3.11] daśakalpasahasrāṇi apy ayas sā mahāniśā*{25}* //" iti. [mbh 13, app. 3.263][3.12-13] anayā khilaśrutyā bhagavato vikhanaśśabdavācyatvaṃ katham avagamyata iti cet ucyate.
 [itihāsapurāṇābhyām eva vedārthasya nirṇeyatvam]

[3.14] "durbodhā vaidikāś śabdā prakīrṇatvāc ca ye khilāḥ /
[3.15] tadjñais ta eva spaṣṭārthāḥ smṛtitantre pratiṣṭhitāḥ //"*{26}* iti

[3.16] "yadi vidyāc caturvedān sāṅgopaniṣadān dvijaḥ /
[3.17] na cet purāṇasadvidyā na vedārthavicakṣaṇaḥ //" iti

[3.18] "itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ vedaṃ samupabṛhmayet*{27}* /
[3.19] bibhety alpaśruvād*{28}* vedo mām ayaṃ pratariṣyati //" iti ca [mbh 1.1.204]

[3.20-21] smaraṇāt itihāsapurāṇābhyām evārthanirṇayaḥ kartavyaḥ. bhārate mokṣadharme nāradastutau:

[3.22-23] "namas te devadeveśa"*{29}* ity ārabhya stotramadhye "phenapācārya vālakhilya vikhano vikhanasa vaikhānasācārya abhagnayoga abhagnaparisaṅkhyāna"*{30}* iti.
[3.24] tatraiva: "yat tasminn upalabhyaṃ te tat tejas tat trayīmayam /
[3.25] tad vaikhānaḥ paraṃ brahma iti vedavido viduḥ //" iti coktam. [mbh ]

!{28}! lies mit mbh: alpaśrutād.
!{29}! mbh 12.325.4a: namas te devadeva.
!{30}! bezug auf mbh 12.325.4j-k: prathamatrisauparṇa [91] pañcāgne [92] triṇāciketa [93] ṣaḍaṅgavidhāna [94] prāgjyotiṣa [95] jyeṣṭhasāmaga [96] sāmikavratadhara [97] atharvaśiraḥ [98] pañcamahākalpa [99] phenapācārya [100] // vālakhily.a [101] vaikhānasa [102] abhagnayoga [103] abhagnaparisaṃkhyāna [104] yugāde [105] yugamadhya [106] yuganidhana [107] ākhaṇḍala [108] prācīnagarbha [109] kauśika [110]; s.u., dhn[d] 10.1-3.

 [vikhanaśśabdanirvacanam]

[4.1-2] tathā nāmasahasrādhyāye "vaikhānas sāmagāyanaḥ"*{31}*" iti smaryate.

 [jagatsṛṣṭiprayojanam]

[4.3] pañcarātre ātmasaṃhitāyām:
[4.4] "mahābhūtena bhūtena vyāptaṃ vikhanasā jagat /
[4.5] tam eva śaraṇaṃ gaccha jagatkāraṇam acyutam //" [ātmasaṃhitā]
[4.6] iti śāṇḍilyena śatānandam abhilakṣyoktam.[4.7] vaikhānase ānandasaṃhitāyāṃ:[4.8] "vedāntatattvamīmāṃsākhananaṃ kṛtavāt hariḥ* /{32}*[4.9] nāmnā vikhanasaṃ prāhur yañ ca vaikhānasaṃ tathā* //{33}*" iti proktam. [ās ][4.10-12] atra khananaśabdena saṅkalpa ucyate. "so 'kāmayata. bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa tapo 'tayata"*{34}* ityādi śrutibhyaḥ. avāptasamastakāmasyāpi bhagavataḥ sṛṣṭikārye pravṛttir bhavati.
 [samaṣṭisṛṣṭilakṣaṇam]

[4.13] nanu satyavādisamastakalyāṇaguṇaviśiṣṭasya bhagavataḥ.
[4.14] "aiśvaryasya samagrasya vīryasya yaśasaḥ śriyaḥ /
[4.15] jñānavairāgyayoś caiva ṣaṇṇāṃ bhaga itīraṇā //"
[4.16] iti samagraṣāḍguṇyaparipūrṇasya avāptasamastakāmasya kimarthaṃ sṛṣṭyadikam*{35}* iti cet ucyate.[4.17] "aprameyo 'niyojyaś ca yatra kāmagamo vaśī / [mbh 2, app. 21.1605][4.18] modate bhagavān bhūtaiḥ bālaḥ kīḍanakair iva* //{36}*" [mbh 2, app. 21.1606][4.19] ityādi bhāratavacanānusāreṇa līlārtham eveti.[4.20] jagadsṛṣṭyādilīlānubhavārthaṃ bhagavatā samaṣṭisṛṣṭer anantaraṃ vyaṣṭisṛṣṭau
[4.21-22] devamanuṣyādivividhaviśeṣasṛṣṭyarthaṃ caturmukhasṛṣṭiṃ prati dhyānaṃ kṛtam. eṣā cidacidātmikā sṛṣṭiḥ bhagavatā kriyate. vyaṣṭisṛṣṭis tu brahmaṇā. samaṣṭisṛṣṭir nāma:
[4.23] "bhūtais tu pañcabhiḥ prāṇaiḥ svāntair daśabhir indriyaiḥ /
[4.24] caturviṃśāti tattvāni sāṅkhyaśāstravido viduḥ //

[5.1] mahān kālaḥ pradhānañ ca māyāvidyā ca pūruṣaḥ /

 [vyaṣṭisṛṣṭilakṣaṇam]

[5.3-9] iti vacanāt tattvasṛṣṭir ity avagamyate. "ajām ekāṃ lohitaśuklakṛṣṇām" "nityo nityānām cetanaś cetanānām". ityādi śrutibhiḥ nityatvena śrutānāṃ prakṛtipuruṣānāṃ sṛṣṭir nāma pralayadaśāyāṃ sūkṣmarūpeṇa avibhaktanāmarūpeṇa ca paramātmany ekībhūtānāṃ sṛṣṭikāle paramātmano 'nupraveśānantaraṃ sthūlarūpavatvaṃ vibhaktanāmarūpabhāktvañ ca. "tat sṛṣṭvā". "tad evānuprāviśat. tad anupraviśya. sac ca tyac cābhavat" ityādi śruteḥ.

[8.1] tatrārcako mahābhāgo bhagavān vikhanās tadā*{65}* /

[8.3] śrīvaikhānase - ānandasaṃhitāyām:
[8.4] "antarhitānāṃ khananād vedānān tu viśeṣataḥ /

[8.7] vyāsanighaṇṭau: "vikhanasañ ca vidhātāraṃ viriñca*{68}* taṃ caturmukham /" iti[8.8] "nābhijanmāṇḍajaḥ pūrvo vikhanāḥ kamalāsanaḥ //[8.9] śatānandaś śatadhṛtis satyako haṃsavāhanaḥ* /{69}*[8.10] padmāsano vikhanasaś cāharmukhaḥ*{70}* itīritaḥ //" iti ca pratipāditam.*{71}*[8.11-12] evaṃ kāryakāraṇayor abhedāvagamāt*{72}* pramāṇabāhulyāc ca bhagavati nārāyaṇe caturmukhe ca vaikhānasaśabdaprayogaprakāraḥ*{73}* pratipāditaḥ.[8.13] vaikhānasānām utpattiprakāraḥ*{74}*

[8.14-23] vaikhānasānām utpattiḥ viśeṣeṇa śrūyate. yajuṣi āruṇaketuke iṣṭakopadhānakathanānuvāke sṛṣṭiprakaraṇe*{75}* - "āpo vā idam āsan*{76}* salilam eva. sa prajāpatir ekaḥ puṣkaraparṇe samabhavat. tasyāntar manasi kāmas samavartata. idaṃ sṛjeyam iti"*{77}* ity ārabhya "sa tapas taptvā. śarīram adhūnuta. tasya yan māṃsam āsīt. tato 'ruṇāḥ ketavo vātaraśanā ṛṣaya udatiṣṭhan.*{78}* ye 'nakhāḥ te vaikhānasāḥ. ye vālāḥ te vālakhilyāḥ."*{79}* iti. asyārthaḥ. samaṣṭisṛṣṭer anantaraṃ vyaṣṭisṛṣṭau caturmukhaḥ*{80}* devamanuṣyādivividhaviśeṣasṛṣṭyarthaṃ matsyādirūpeṇāvatariṣyamāṇasya*{81}* bhagavato nārāyaṇasya paramavaidikatvena sampratipannaśrīvaikhānasabhagavacchāstramārgeṇa*{82}* samārādhdanarthañ ca svātmatulyāḥ prajās sambhaveyur iti svāntaryāmiṇaṃ paramātmānaṃ dhyonenānukṛtavān*{83}* ayam evārtho brāhmāṇḍe 'py ucyate
[8.24] "om ity ekākṣaraṃ brahma vyāharan saṃsmaran harim /
[8.25] padmāsanastho bhagavān paramaṃ tapa āsthitaḥ //" [brahmāṇḍap ]

!{65}! dhn[d] 26.6 liest mit dhn[t] 87: tathā.                   

 [sanakādisṛṣṭiprakāraḥ]

[9.1-5] ity ārabhya*{84}* brahmaṇā brahuśaḥ*{85}* kṛtaṃ tapaścaraṇam uktam. tapaścaraṇakāle sākṣātkṛtabhagavatsvarūpavaibhavānubhavātiśayāt bhagavaddattasṛṣṭiśaktilābhāt tadupajanitaviśeṣavegāc ca pulakitasarvāṅgaḥ śarīram adhūnuta - kampam akarot. "tasya yan māṃsam āsīd"*{86}* māṃsaṃ mānasam iti yāvat. "arthāt prakaraṇāl liṅgād aucityād arthanirṇayaḥ" ity arthādibhiḥ*{87}* samīcīnārthanirṇayavidhānāt "akṣarasāmyān nirbrūyād"*{88}* iti niruktavidhānāñ ca.

[9.6-10] tathā ca tasya manaḥ paramātmani saṃsaktam āsīd iti yat, tena hetunā tadanugrahas samajani. tenānugṛhītāt brahmaṇaḥ "ketavo vātaraśanāḥ ṛṣayaḥ udatiṣṭhan"*{89}*. "aruṇāḥ" paramātmani vasantaḥ taditararaviktāḥ "ketavaḥ" ucchritasvabhāvāḥ paramātmapravaṇānām agresarāḥ "vātaraśanā" digvāsasaḥ "ṛṣayaḥ" sarvārthadarśinaḥ sanakādayaḥ "udatiṣṭhan" utkṛṣya samabhavan iti.*{90}*
[9.11] idaṃ viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi: "sanandanādayo ye ca pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭās tu vedhasā /
[9.12] na te lokeṣv asajjanta nirapekṣāḥ prajāvidhau* //{91}* [viṣṇup 1.7.9]

[9.13] sarve te yogino jātā*{92}* vītarāgā vimatsarāḥ /
[9.14] teṣv evaṃ nirapekṣeṣu lokasṛṣṭau mahātmanaḥ //" ityādinā pratipāditam.*{93}* [viṣṇup 1.7.10]

[9.15-19] sa prajāpatiḥ evaṃvidhān svakāryāsādhakān tān dṛṣṭvā kiñcid viṣādam āpannaḥ punar api svakāraṇaṃ bhagavantaṃ dhyānaprayāyeṇa khananenātoṣat. "ye nakhā" ityādi*{94}*. bhagavadanugrahavikasite prajāpater manasi vaikhānasā nāma ṛṣayas sambhūtāḥ atra "ye nakhā" ity atra ādyantavarṇaviparyayo bhavati. "kaśyapaḥ paśyako bhavatī"tivat "khanā ity etat nakhā" iti viparyastam iti yāvat.*{95}*
[9.20] "suptiṅupagrahaliṅganarāṇāṃ kālahalacsvarakartṛyaṅañ*{96}* ca /
[9.21] vyatyayam icchiti*{97}* śāstrakṛd eṣāṃ so 'pi ca siddhyati bāhulakena //"
[9.22-24] iti, "bahulaṃ chandasī"*{98}*ti cātra praṇāman*{99}*. atra "anakhā" iti cchittvā kecid evam ūcuḥ*{100}*. anakhā ity anena saumyendriyavatvaṃ uktam iti*{101}*.
!{84}! dhn[t] 93 ins. "śūdrajātiṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ paśūnām aśvam eva" cetyantaṃ (evaṃ?).                  

 [vaikhānasānām ācāryapuruṣatvam]
[10.1-3] evañ ca sati "saumyaṃ jitendriyaṃ"*{102}* "suprasannendriyaṃ"*{103}* ityādinā bhagavacchāstreṣv ācāryalakṣaṇasya*{104}* pratipāditatvāt "vaikhānasa vikhanasācarya"*{105}* iti. viṣṇor*{106}* ācāryatvena śāntyparvaṇy abhihitatvāt.[10.4] "vikhanā iti viṣṇus tajjā vaikhānasāḥ smṛtāḥ* /{107}* [kra 36.28cd][10.5] viṣṇor eva samutpannā bhṛgvādyā munayas tathā //"
 [vaikhānasānām triśuklatvam]
[10.6-7] iti vacanāt, "guros sānavṛttir*{108}* vaikhānasa"*{109}* iti bodhāyanasūtre uktatvāc ca bhāgavatādiṣu*{110}* pratipāditam "ācāryapuṃstvam eteṣāṃ vaikhānasānām*{111}* eve"ty avagamyate.
[10.8-9] yadvā "anaghā" iti pāṭhaḥ. anena*{112}* triśuklatvaṃ sūcyate. janma vidyā karma ceti. advārakatvena bhagavataḥ caturmukhāc coptattiśravaṇāt*{113}*,
[10.10] "tatkarma yan na bandhāya sā vidyā yā vimuktaye /

[10.14] "yeṣāṃ trīṇy avadātāni yonirvidyā ca karma ca /

[10.23] loke vihartum icchāmi yad ahaṃ*{118}* padmasambhava /[10.24] tatas tvatsṛṣṭajagatām avicchinnapravṛttaye /[11.1] dharmasaṃrakṣaṇārthāya vedaśāstrārthasiddhaye* //{119}* [ās 4.9]

[18.25] brahmaṇo 'psarasaṃ dṛṣṭvā retaś caskanda karhicit //

!{201}! mbh: ahaṃ vaktā ca mantrasya hotā śukrasya caiva ha.          

[19.1] tat pratīkṣya sa parṇena saṃjuhāva vibhāv asau /
[19.2] tato 'rciṣo 'bhūd bhagavān bhṛgur aṅgārato 'ṅgirāḥ //

[19.3] atraivānveṣaṇād atriḥ khananād vikhanā muniḥ /
[19.4] khananaṃ tattvamīmāṃsety bis hier teluguāhuḥ kecana sūrayaḥ //

[19.5] apare nigamārthānāṃ khananād iti naśśrutam /
[19.6] tatas tadvaṃśajā viprā vedavedāṅgavedinaḥ //" iti.
[19.7-10] "ye vālāḥ te vālakhilyāḥ" ity atra bakārasthāne vakāra*{211}*. jñānātiśayavaibhavāt kāmādidoṣarāhityena ca bālā ucyante. śrūyate hi*{212}*: "tasmād brāhmaṇaḥ pāṇḍityaṃ nirvidya bālyena tiṣṭhāset*{213}* bālyañ ca pāṇdityañ ca nirvidyātha muniḥ" iti.[19.11-13] atra kecid evam ūcuḥ: brahmaṇaḥ vidhūtāc charīrāt yanmāṃsaṃ vikīrṇam abhavat tato ketavo vātaraśanā ṛṣaya udatiṣṭhann iti. tad asat. evam arthasvīkāre sṛṣṭikāraṇabhūtasya brahmaśarīrasya śaithilyam uktaṃ syād iti.[19.14-20] kiñ ca "tasyāntarmanasi kāmas samavartata" ityādinā "kāmas tadagre samavartatādhi" ity antena sopapattikaṃ vartamānaṃ saṅkalparūpaṃ mananavyāpāram uktvā "manaso retaḥ prathamaṃ yad āsīd" ity atra tatra vidyamānasya vyāpārasya prajāpateḥ sṛṣṭikāraṇatvaṃ retaś śabdebis hier telugunoktvā "sato bandhum asati niravindann" ity ārabhya "ya evaṃ veda" ity antena brahmaṇas tatkālavidyamānamānasaśaktimāab hier telugutreṇa vyaṣṭisṛṣṭer aniṣpannatvam uktvā manaso vyaṣṭikāraṇalābhāya "sa tapo 'tapyata" iti bhagavadupāsanam akarod" ity uktam. ayam evārthaḥ "oṃ ity ekākṣaraṃ brahme"tyādinā brahmāṇḍe 'py uktam.*{214}*
 [bhrgvādīnāṃ bhagavanmānasaputratvam]

[19.21] bhagavanmānasaputrā bhṛgvādaya iti bhagavataivoktam:
[19.22] "maharṣayas sapta pūrve catvāro manavas tathā /
[19.23] madbhāvā mānasā jātā yeṣāṃ loka imāḥ prajāḥ //" [mbh 6.32.6]

 [bhṛgvādīnāṃ vaikhānasavaṃśakartṛtvam]

!{211}! dhn[t] 120: bakārasya sthāne vakāraḥ.    
[20.1] yathā śāntiparvaṇi:[20.2] "bhṛgvaṅgiromarīcyatri pulastyapulahāḥ kratuḥ*{215}* / [mbh 13, app. 7.49][20.3] tathā vasiṣṭho dakṣaś ca nava svāyambhuvā dvijāḥ* //{216}*
[20.4] ete vaikhānasānān tu ṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanāṃ /

[20.6-8] tasmād bhagavatā nārāyaṇena brahmaṇā ca sṛṣṭānāṃ bhṛgvādīnām ṛṣīṇāṃ tadvaṃśajānāṃ ca niṣekādikriyāvatām advārakabhagavadyajanādhikāravatām eva loke vaikhānasā iti prasiddhiḥ.
 [caturmukhasṛṣṭānāṃ sarveṣāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ vaikhānasatvaṃ samānam ity ākṣepasya parihāraḥ]

[20.9] nanu brahmaṇā sṛṣṭānāṃ sarveṣām api manuṣyānāṃ vaikhānasatvaṃ samānam.
[20.10-11] katham eteṣv eva vyavahriyate iti cet satyam. nāmarūbis hier telugupakṛtyavibhāgādikaṃ vedaśabdebhya eva brahmaṇā kṛtam iti śrūyate. "vedena nāmarūpe vyākarot satāsatī*{217}* prajāpatir" iti.
[20.12] tathā bhārate: "anādinidhanā hy eṣā vāgudsṛṣṭā svayambhuvā* //{218}* [mbh 12.224.55cd]

[20.16] manu: "sarveṣāñ ca sa nāmāni karmāṇi ca pṛthak pṛthak /

[20.18-19] iti ca nāmarūpavibhāgasya śrutismṛtiṣu pratipāditatvāt brahmaṇā tādṛśaśrutismṛtyanusāreṇa sṛṣṭānām eva vaikhānasatvavyavahāraḥ. nānyeṣām.
[20.20-23] kiñca ekasmin paramapuruṣe mukhādiṣu jātānāṃ yathā brāhmaṇādivyavahāraḥ yathā viśvāmitra bhāradvājādi gotreṣūtpannānām ekasūtraniṣṭhatvaṃ vinā anekasūtrānusāritvaṃ, yathā ca kumudakahlārādiṣu "paṅke jāyata" iti vyutpattyā paṅkajatve samāno 'pi yogarūḍhibhyāṃ paṅkajatvaṃ tāmarasa eva vartate tathaiva vaikhānasatvam api. tathoktam:
[20.24] "kalpe kalpe kṣayotpattyā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ /

[26.14] tathā āgneyapurāṇe phullāraṇyamāhātmye:
[26.15] "phullaśiṣyās tu yakṣās te pūjayanti yuge yuge /
[26.16] vaikhānasena vidhinā yathā phullamukhāc cyutam // [agnip ]
[26.17] mānuṣāḥ pūjayantīha vaikhānasamate sthitāḥ //" iti [agnip ]
[26.18] tathā brahmakaivarte puṣkaratīrthavaibhavavarṇane:
[26.19] "nimnagānāṃ yathā gaṅgā devānāṃ bhagavān hariḥ /
[26.20] varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇāś śreṣṭhā āśramāṇāṃ yatir yathā // [brahmakaivartap ]

[26.21] śrutīnām ādibhūtānām ādir ekāyanī yathā /
[26.22] vyūhānām ādibhūtas tu vāsudevo yathā varaḥ /
[26.23] trimūrtīnāṃ yathā viṣṇuś śivānān tu sadāśivaḥ* //{261}* [brahmakaivartap ]

 [vipreṣu vaikhānasānāṃ, sūtreṣu vaikhānasasūtrasya ca śreṣṭhyam]

[27.1] sūtrāṇāṃ tatpraṇītan tu yathā śreṣṭhatamaṃ smṛtam /

[27.3-6] iti ca pratipādanāt īdṛśānāṃ vaikhānasānām eva śrutismṛtītihāsapurāṇādiṣu caturmukhāt sāmānyatvena vinā sarvotkṛṣṭatvenotpattiśravaṇāt brahmasabhāpraveśasūryapathādyāśrayaṇādipratipādanāc ca vaikhānasā na tṛtīyāśramaniṣṭhāḥ, na vā brahmaṇā sāmānyataḥ sṛṣṭā bhavitum arhanti.
 [jambudvīpe bhāratavarśasya śreṣṭhyam]

 [vānaprasthānāṃ mukhyavṛttyā vaikhānasaśabdavācyatvābhāvaḥ]

[42.9] yathā munīnāṃ vikhanā ādibhūta udāhṛtaḥ* /{359}*[42.10] sūtrāṇāṃ tatpraṇītan tu yathā śreṣṭhatamaṃ smṛtam // [brahmakaivarta.p ][42.11] tathaiva puṣkaro rājaṃs tīrthānām uttamottamaḥ //"*{360}* [brahmakaivartap ]

[42.13] "maccittā madgataprāṇā mayi saṅgatamānasāḥ /
[42.14] ananyaśaraṇā rājaṃs tasmād vaikhānasā varāḥ* //{361}*" [kūrmap ]

 [vaikhānasādhiṣṭhatadeśe viṣṇusānnidhyam]

[42.15] purāṇāntare:
[42.16] "yatra vaikhānasā viprā yatra santi gavāṃ gaṇāḥ /
[42.17] yatra bilvāḥ palāśāś ca tatra sannihito hariḥ* //{362}*"

[42.18] bṛhannāradīye:
[42.19] "jagatpavitrās te nityaṃ viṣṇum abhyarcayanti ye /
[42.20] durvṛttā vā suvṛttā vā pūjanīyā viśeṣataḥ //" [bṛhannāradap]
[42.21] hārīte:[42.22] tasmāt te śuddhasattvasthāś śuddhā vaikhānasāḥ smṛtāḥ* /{363}*[42.23] yān lokān prāpnuvanty ete tān śṛṇuṣva samāhitaḥ //"[42.24] pāñcarātre pauṣkare:[42.25] "viprā vaikhānasākhyā ye te bhaktās tattvam ucyate* //{364}* [pauṣkaras 36.260cd][42.26] ekāntinas susattvasthā dehāntaṃ nānyayājinaḥ /
!{359}! diese zeile fehlt im zitat in dhn[d] 26.19-27.2.      
[43.1] kartavyam iti deveśaṃ saṃyajante phalaṃ vinā* //{365}* [pauṣkaras 36.261][43.2] prāpnuvanti ca dehānte vāsudevatvam abjaja //" iti*{366}* [pauṣkaras 36.262ab]

 [puṣkare vaikhānasāśramaḥ]

 [vaikhānasānām pūjanīyatvam]

[43.23] pañcavaikhānasāṃś caiva viprādīṃś caturas tathā /
[43.24] pañcayogaratādyāṃs tu tathānyān vaiṣṇavān dvijān* //{375}* [pārameśvaras 12.438]

 [vaikhānasetarasūtriṇāṃ pañcakālaparāyaṇatvābhavāḥ]

[46.1-5] itthaṃ vāsudevādīnāṃ daivikamānuṣabhedena dvaividhyasya, "puruṣaṃ paramapuruṣaṃ paramātmānaṃ paraṃ brahmāṇam" ityādinā pratipāditānāṃ caturṇāṃ puruṣādīnāṃ mūrtivibhāgasya ca śrīvaikhānasaśāstre pratipādanāt, etas sarvavibhāgajña eva caturvyūhavibhāgavid ity anenocyate. ācchidrapañcakālajña iti:*{387}*
[46.6] "prātaḥkāle 'bhigamanam upādānaṃ tataḥ param /
[46.7] madhyāhna ijyāṃ kurvīta svādhyāyañ cāparāhṇake /
[46.8] yogaṃ sāyāhnakāle tu pañcakālā udāhṛtāḥ //" [va ]
[46.9] iti vāsādhikāre pratipāditapañcakālaparāyaṇam adhikṛtya prakṛttāni*{388}* -[46.10-14] "ye pāvayanti dharaṇīṃ" "ijyāmadhye tathāhome" "ye toṣayanty avirataṃ" iti vacanāni, sāmanyena pañcakālaparāyaṇasya darśanasparśanādibhis sarveṣāṃ pāvanatāṃ kṛtārthatāṃ, ijyāyogādisamayeṣu cāgatasya tasya pūjanāntaraṃ śeṣakarmācaraṇañ ca pratipādayanti, etādṛśaḥ pañcakālaparāyaṇaḥ kīdṛśā ity ākaṅkṣāyāṃ "dvādaśākṣaratattvajña" ityādinā "acchidrapañcakālajña" ity antena tallakṣaṇam ucyate.[46.15-17] īdṛśācchidrapañcakālaparāyaṇā vaikhānasā eva. vaikhānasaśāstra eva pañcakālavibhāgasya pratipāditatvāt. svasvasūtre 'nuktatvād āpastambīyādayas tu na. pañcakālapratipādanarahitasūtrāntaraniṣṭhānāṃ:*{389}*[46.18] "brāhme muhūrte buddhyeta dharmārthāv anucintayan* /{390}*" ity ārabhya[46.19] "dvitīye ca tathā bhāge vedābhyāso vidhīyate //
[46.20] tṛtīye ca tathā bhāge poṣyavargārthacintanam /
[46.21] bhāge caturthe kurvīta snānam ambhasy akṛtrime //

[46.22] pañcame tu tathā bhāge saṃvibhāgo yathārhataḥ /
[46.23] itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ ṣaṣṭaṃ saptamam abhyaset /
[46.24] aṣṭame lokayātrāñ ca vicārya ca gṛhī tataḥ //"

!{387}! dhn[t] 188-189 statt dhn[d] 46.1-5: itthaṃ vāsudevādīnāṃ vyūhabhūtāṇāṃ daivikamānuṣabhedena vyūhacaturmūrtipratipādanāt "puruṣaṃ paramapuruṣaṃ paramātmānaṃ paraṃ brahmāṇam" ityādinā caturṇāṃ puruṣādīnāṃ mūrtivibhāgasya ca śrīvaikhānasaśāstre pratipāditatvāt. "acchidrapañcakālajñaḥ".

[47.3] anyathā
[47.4] "vidharmaḥ paradharmaś ca ābhāsa upa vā cchalaḥ*{392}* /
[47.5] adharmaśākhāḥ pañcemā dharmajño 'dharmavattyajet //

[47.6] dharmabādho vidharmas syāt paradharmo 'nyacoditaḥ /
[47.7] upadharmas tu pāṣaṇḍo dambhovāṃśasurbhiśchalaḥ (?)*{393}* /

[47.9] iti bhāgavatavacanoktaparadharmāśrayaṇadoṣaprasaṅgaḥ*{394}*.

[47.11] svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmo bhayāvahaḥ* //{395}*" [mbh 6.25.35]

 [sūtrāntaranuṣṭhānāṃ pāñcarātrānuyāyināñ ca devalakatvam]
[47.13-19] kiñca tatsūtreṣu dvādaśākṣaratattvādipratipādanam api nāsti. evaṃ "sati kuḍye citrakarme"ti nyāyena yajñopavītadhāraṇasandhyopāsanabhagavadārādhanādividhipratipādanarahitasūtrāntaraniṣṭhānāṃ, tathā śrīmannārāyaṇasya samānatvena rudrādidevatāntarārādhanavidhipratipādakasūtraniṣṭhānāñ ca caturvyūhavibhāgajñānāsambhavāt bhagavadārādhanasvarūpajñānābhāvena pañcakālaparāyaṇatvādigandhaleśo 'pi na sambhavati. sūtrāntaroktamārgeṇa vā pañcarātroktamārgeṇa vā bhagavadārādhanaṃ kurvato 'nadhikāriṇo devalakatvaṃ pratipādyate.*{397}*
 [pāñcarātre durgādidevatāntarārcanapratipādanam]

[48.1] "kuryāt pāśāṅkuśau vāpi śaṅkhacakrāv athāpi vā* /{401}*[48.2] ākhuṃ vāpi khagendraṃ vā tasya vāhanam ācaret* //{402}* [viṣvaksenas ][48.3] nārāyaṇāśakatvāc cāvyāvṛttatvān mahāmune* /{403}*[48.4] vīśas tadvāhanaṃ proktaṃ ākhuṃ vāpi samācaret // [viṣvaksena.s ]

 [vaikhānasavyatiriktānāṃ paramaikāntitvābhāvaḥ]

[48.16-17] atra "yair iṣṭaḥ pañcakālajñair" ity anena pañcakālavyatiriktakālāntarapratipādakaśāstraniṣṭhānāṃ*{406}* vyavṛttiḥ. "ekāntibhir narair" ity anena

[49.13] utthāyāsīta śayane kīrtayan nāma vaiṣṇavam /

[52.1] ity ācamanasya mahāniśāyāṃ niṣedhāt.*{443}*[52.2] "yāmadvayaṃ śayānas tu brahmabhūyāya kalpate //"[52.3-4] iti dharmaśāstroktanidrākāle yogasyāyuktatvāc ca. yogakālasyārdharātrikatve svādhyāyakālād vyavahitatvena chidrapāñcakālikatvāpātāc ca.*{444}*[52.5-6] kālacatuṣtvāsyaivoktatvena abhigamanādiṣv ekasya lopasambhavena aniyatapañcakālaparasya pañcakālaparāyaṇaśabdābhilāpāsambhavāc ca.*{445}*

[52.24-53.2] iti devatāpūjakasya devalakatvaṃ sambhavatīti cet - tad asat. sāmānyataḥ devatārādhanaṃ ye kurvanti te devalakā iti vā? uta śrutismṛtītihāsapurāṇādiṣu mukhyādhikāritvena pratipāditā apīti vā?. sāmānyataḥ devatārādhanaṃ ye kurvanti te iti cet - tarhi gṛhadevatāpūjakānām api devalakatvaprasaṅgaḥ. kiñca:*{451}*

 [vaikhānasānām devalakatvābhāvaḥ]
[53.3] "brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca vipro vaikhānasas tathā* /{452}*[53.4] kurvanti*{453}* nijakarmāṇi viṣṇum eva yajanti te //"[53.5-11] iti sandhyopāsanādīnāṃ bhagavadārādhanarūpatvoktyā*{454}* teṣāñ ca tyāgas sambhavati. atas sāmānyataḥ iti*{455}* vaktum ayuktam. śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu*{456}* mukhyādhikāritvena pratipāditā devalakāḥ*{457}* iti cet - tad asat. "'agnir vai devānām avamo viṣṇuḥ paramas tadantareṇa sarvā anyā devatā'; iti brāhmaṇam. tasmād gṛhe paramaṃ viṣṇuṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sāyaṃ prātar homānte 'rcayati" iti vaikhānasasūtre*{458}*, "pravaḥ pāntam andhaso dhiyāyate maheśūrāya viṣṇave cārcata"*{459}* iti ṛgbrāhmaṇam anusṛtya*{460}* viṣṇupradhānatayā "sa vā eṣa puruṣaḥ pañcadhā pañcātmā" ityādiśrutyuktaviṣṇvādipañcamūrtīnām*{461}* ārādhanasya pratipāditatvāt*{462}*.[53.12-13] āśvamedhike "kathaṃ tvam arcanīyo 'sī"*{463}*tyādeḥ, vṛddhamanau "vedāntavedibhir"*{464}* ityādeś coktatvāt.[53.14-15] evam eva pāñcarātraśaivaśilpajyautiṣādiṣu utkṛṣṭamukhyādhikāripratipādakānāṃ vacanānāṃ vaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt tanmūlabhūtaśrutismṛtipurāṇādīnām aprāmāṇyaprasaṅgo duṣpariharaḥ.*{465}*
 [vaikhānasānām bhagavaddravyopabhogādau doṣābhāvaḥ]
[53.16-17] evaṃ ca pramāṇabhūteṣu śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu pratipāditānām ācārādīnāṃ tyāgaḥ prasajyet, niṣphalatvāt. nanu paradravyoṇālayārcanaṃ*{466}* kurvatāṃ devalakatvam iti cet na.*{467}*[53.18-19] śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu tattacchāstreṣu ca ālayārcakānāṃ*{468}* mukhyādhikāritvena taddravyopabhogārhatvena ca pratipādanāt.*{469}*
[53.20] yathā - marīciproktāyām ānandasaṃhitāyāṃ vikhanasotpattyādikaṃ pratipādya:
[53.21] "tathā tvadanujīvitve tvaddravyānubhave sati /

[56.18] ṛtvijān tu tadardhaṃ syāt tadardham itarasya ca //"
[56.19] iti dakṣiṇādānaṃ pratipādyate.*{507}*[56.20] nanu - "pratigraheṇa viprasya brāhmaṃ tejo vinaśyati* //{508}*" iti manuvacanāt*{509}* [manudhś 4.186cd][56.21-25] "pratigraheṇa tejo hi viprāṇāṃ śāmyate" ity ānuśāsanikavacanāc ca pratigraheṇa brahmatejonāśanaṃ smaryate. śrūyate pratigrahe prāyaścittam api. "yo yājayati prati vā gṛhṇāti yājayitvā pratigṛhya vānaśnaṃs tris svādhyāyam adhīyīta trirātraṃ sāvitrīṃ gāyatrīm anvatirecayati varo dakṣiṇā vareṇaiva varaṃ spṛṇoty ātmā hi varaḥ" iti.[56.25] ataḥ pratigrahe doṣo 'stīti cet - na.*{510}*

 [harismaraṇasya mokṣapradatvam]

[57.1] "trāyante khalu nātyantam anyadharmās svanuṣṭitāḥ /
[57.2] api matkarma viguṇaṃ trāyate mahato bhayāt //

[57.3] merumandaramātro 'pi rāśiḥ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ /
[57.4] keśavaṃ vaidyam āsādya ab hier noch telugu vergleichendurvyādhir iva naśyati //

[57.5] nidhisthānaṃ khanan dveṣāt mṛdarthaṃ vāpnuyān nidhim /
[57.6] ajñaḥ kāmāc ca doṣāc ca smṛtvaivaṃ mokṣabhāktathā //

[57.7] dveṣiṇā vāprayatnena kṣipto 'gniḥ kakṣamādahet /
[57.8] katham abhyarcito viṣṇuḥ na dahet sarvakilbiṣam //

[57.9] yathājño vajrakāyas syāt spardhann api sudhāṃ piban /
[57.10] evaṃ viruddhabhāvo 'pi mucyaty eva hariṃ smaran //" iti

[57.11] nāradīye: "kṛtāpi dambhahāsyādyair yat sevā tārayej janān /
[57.12] viphalā nānyakarmeva kṛpāluḥ ko 'nvataḥ param // [nāradap.]

[57.13] hāsyānādaramāyābhir api bhaktiḥ kṛtā tvayi /
[57.14] nṛṇāṃ dadātīndrapadaṃ sāttvikānāṃ kim ucyate // [nāradap]

[57.15] vastusvabhāva evaiṣa yanmokṣāya harismṛtiḥ /
[57.16] pūṣeva dhyāntanāśāya śśītaśāntyai yathānalaḥ // [nāradap.]

[57.17] saiṣā harismṛtiṛ daityaṃ krodhād api kṛtā satī /
[57.18] ānayet sadgatiṃ vipraṃ sānugaṃ kimu varṇyate // [nāradap.]

[57.19] yathāmṛtārthaṃ yatatāṃ surāṇām abdhimanthane /
[57.20] pārijātādikāny āsan phalāny aprārthitāny api // [nāradap.]

[57.21] evaṃ mokṣaikacittānāṃ yatatām īśasaṃsmṛtau /
[57.22] bhavanti siddhayo divyāḥ puṇya*{511}* puṇyānubandhi yat //" ityādi [nāradap]

[57.23] tatraiva: "surātithyarcanakṛte gurubhṛtyartham eva ca /
[57.24] sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyāt na tu duṣyet svayaṃ tataḥ //" [nāradap]

!{511}! lies: puṇyaṃ. 
[58.1-2] iti ca smaraṇāt. ataḥ śāstroktamārgeṇa bhagavadyajanavidhau pravṛttānāṃ tattatkarmasu dakṣiṇāpratigrahe kṛte 'pi na doṣaḥ.
 [ālayārcanāyāḥ mahābhāratādisaṃmatatvam]
[58.3] gṛhārcanāvyatirekeṇālayārcanā bhāratādiṣu pratipāditā dṛśyate. yathā -[58.4] mahābhārate āśvamedhike "kathaṃ tvam arcanīyo 'sī"ty ādi. [mbh 14 app. 4.1652pr]
[58.5] viṣṇudharmottare ṣaṣṭhe 'dhyāye:
[58.6] "yas tu devagṛhasyārthaṃ prākāraṃ parikalpayet /
[58.7] sa tu svargaṃ samāsadya vimānādhipatir bhavet // [viṣṇudharmottara.p ]

[58.8] yas tu devālayasyāgre śilādārubhir eva vā /
[58.9] karoti toraṇaṃ ramyaṃ sa tu svargādhipo bhavet // [viṣṇudharmottara.p ]

[58.10] yas tu devālayaṃ viṣṇor dāruśailamṛdā tathā /
[58.11] iṣṭakākalpitaṃ vāpi kuryāt tasya phalaṃ bahu // [viṣṇudharmottara.p ]

[58.12] ahanyahany aśvamedha- sahasrāṇi karoti yaḥ /
[58.13] prāpnoti maṇḍapaṃ viṣṇoḥ yaḥ kārayati mānavaḥ // [viṣṇudharmottara.p ]

[58.14] keśavasya sa tallokam akṣayyaṃ pratipadyate /
[58.15] pratimārthaṃ mahāviṣṇos sādhayed uttamāṃ śilām // [viṣṇudharmottarap ]
[58.16] ṣaṣṭirvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate //" iti. [viṣṇudharmottarap ][58.17-19] eteṣāṃ ca prākāratoraṇamaṇḍapavigrahaśilādīṇāṃ gṛhadevatāsvasaṃbhavaḥ śrīvaikhānasasaṃhitāsu pratipāditaḥ. prasaṅgād arcakamahimādīha kathyate.
 [arcakamāhātmyam]
[58.20] bṛhannāradīye: "sa kadācin mahāpāpo jantūnāmantakopamaḥ //" [bṛhannāradap]
[58.21] ity ārabhya
[58.22] "tasyopavanamadhyasthaṃ ramyaṃ keśavamandiram /
[58.23] chāditaṃ hemakavacaiḥ dṛṣṭvā vyādho mudā yayau // [bṛhannāradap]

[58.24] harāmy atra suvarṇāni bahūnīti sa niścitaḥ /
[58.25] jagāma viṣṇubhavanaṃ kīnāśaś cauryalolupaḥ // [bṛhannāradap]

[59.1] tatrāpaśyad dvijavaraṃ śāntaṃ tattvārthakovidam /
[59.2] paricaryāparaṃ viṣṇor udaṅkaṃ tapasāṃ nidhim // [bṛhannāradap]

[59.3] ekāntinaṃ dayāluñ ca nisspṛhaṃ dhyānalolupam /
[59.4] dṛṣṭvā taṃ lubdhako mene svakāryasyāntarāyinam // [bṛhannāradap]
[59.5] devasya dravyajātan tu samādātumanā niśi //" [bṛhannāradap][59.6-7] ityādināpṛthagālayārcakasadbhāvādikaṃ uktvā svakāryāntarāya bhūtārcakahiṃsāyāṃ pravṛttasya tasya maraṇam api pratipādya.
 [viṣṇupādodakamāhātmyam]

[59.8] "udaṅkaḥ patitaṃ prekṣya lubdhakantu dayāparaḥ /
[59.9] viṣṇupādodakenainam abhyaṣiñ canmahāmuniḥ //

[59.10] haripādodakas parśāl lubdhako vītakalmaṣaḥ /
[59.11] divyaṃ vimānamāruhya munim enam athābravīt //"
[59.12] iti bhagavatpādodakamāhātmyaṃ ca pratipāditam.[59.13] tatraiva - yajñadhvajavītihotrasaṃvāde:
 [ālaye dīpasthāpanādeḥ phalam]

[59.14] "sa kadācit tu kāmāndho rantukāmaḥ parastriyam /
[59.15] śūnyaṃ pūjādibhir viṣṇor mandiraṃ prāptavān niśi //

[59.16] tatra kāmopabhogārthaṃ śayituṃ tena kāminā /
[59.17] svavastraprāntato brahman kṛtaṃ taddeśamārjanam //

[59.18] yāvantaḥ pāṃsukaṇikāḥ tena sammārjitās tadā /
[59.19] tāvaj janmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tadaiva kṣayam āgatam //

[59.20] pradīpaḥ sthāpitas tatra suratārthaṃ dvijottama /
[59.21] tenāpi tasya duṣkarma niśśeṣaṃ kṣayam āgatam //

[59.22] avaśenāpi yatkarma kṛtvemāṃ siddhim āgataḥ /
[59.23] bhaktimadbhiḥ praśāntaiś ca kiṃ punas samyagarcanāt //

 [ālayapradakṣiṇaphalam]

[60.1] tasmāc chruṇuta viprendrāḥ devo nārāyaṇo 'vyayaḥ /
[60.2] jñānato 'jñānato vāpi pūjakānāṃ vimuktidaḥ //"

[60.3] tathā tatraiva - indrasudharmasaṃvāde:
[60.4] "ahamāsaṃ purā śakra gṛdhraḥ pāpāvaśeṣataḥ /
[60.5] sthitaś ca bhūmibhāge vai amedhyāmiṣabhojanaḥ //

[60.6] ekadāhaṃ viṣṇugṛhe prākāre saṃsthitaḥ prabhoḥ /
[60.7] patito vyādhaśastreṇa sāyaṃ viṣṇugṛhaṃ gate //

[60.8] mayi kaṇṭhagataprāṇe kaścit śvā māṃsalolupaḥ /
[60.9] jagraha māṃ svavaktreṇa śvabhir anyair abhidrutaḥ //

[60.10] gataḥ pradakṣiṇākāraṃ viṣṇos tanmandiraṃ prabhoḥ /
[60.11] tenaiva tuṣṭim āpannaḥ antarātmā jaganmayaḥ //

[60.12] mama cāpi śunaś cāpi dattavān paramaṃ padam /
[60.13] pradakṣiṇākāratabis hier noch telugu vergleichenyā gatasya sadṛśaṃ phalam //

[60.14] samprāptaṃ tu mayā śakra*{512}* kiṃ punas samyag arcanāt /
[60.15] ye 'rcayanti sadā bhaktyā nārāyaṇam anāmayam /
[60.16] tān arcayanti vibudhā brahmādyā devatāgaṇāḥ //"*{513}* iti

 [amedhyāni pañca]
[60.17] evam āśvamedhike: "loke trīṇy apavitrāṇi pañcāmedhyāni bhārata / [mbh 13, app. 4.3249][60.18] śvā ca śūdraś śvapākaś ca tryapavitrāṇi pāṇḍava* /{514}* [mbh 13, app. 4.3250][60.19] devalaḥ kukkuṭo yūpaḥ udakyā vṛṣalīpatiḥ //" [mbh 13, app. 4.3251][60.20] pañcamedhyāni*{515}* iti.
 [bhagavatpūjādyanadhikāriṇaḥ]

!{512}! dhn[t] 253: samprāptaṃ vibudhaśreṣṭha.    
[61.1] nārhanti tasmāt kurvīta dvāraṃ yavanikāvṛtam //"[61.2-3] iti pratipādanāt bhagavadarcanadarśanādiṣu yogyatārahitānāṃ nikṛṣṭānāṃ (devalakānāṃ) autkṛṣṭyaṃ na sambhavati.*{516}*
 [advārakabhagavadyājinām utkṛṣṭatvam]

[61.4-6] śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣūktaprakāreṇa kalpasūtre*{517}* yeṣām advārakabhagavadyajanādhikāro vidhīyate te utkṛṣṭā jñeyāḥ*{518}*. yathā śrutiḥ: "yathā kratur asmin loke bhavati tathetaḥ pretya bhavati"*{519}* iti.
[61.7] smṛtiś ca*{520}*: "vedoktenaiva bhārgeṇa*{521}* sarvabhūtahṛdi sthitam /
[61.8] mām arcayanti ye bhaktās*{522}* sāyujyaṃ yānti te mama //

[61.9] tasmād yāvaj jano jīvet tāvat sampūjayed dharim /
[61.10] pāpair na lipyate martyo*{523}* harimandiram āpnuyāt //

[61.11] jagat pavitrās te nityaṃ viṣṇum abhyarcayanti ye /
[61.12] durvṛttā vā suvṛttā vā pūjanīyā viśeṣataḥ //"

 [vaikhānasānāṃ bhagavatprītipātratvam]
[61.13-16] vyāsenapi*{524}* ānuśāsanike (90. adhyāye) pātrakathanāvasare*{525}* devalakānām apātratāṃ satkarmaniṣṭhānāṃ pātratāñ ca pratipādya svavacanadṛḍhīkaraṇārthaṃ "vaikhānasā vā ṛṣaya indrasya priyā āsan"*{526}* iti bhagavatprītiviṣayāṇāṃ*{527}* vaikhānasānāṃ vacanam api śrūyate iti pratipāditam. yathā:[61.17] *{528}*"ṛṣīṇāṃ samayaṃ nityaṃ ye rakṣanti yudhiṣṭhira* /{529}*[61.18] niścitāḥ sarvadharmajñās tān devā brāhmaṇān viduḥ // [mb.h 13.9.42]
[61.19] svādhyāyaniṣṭhā ṛṣayo*{530}* jñānaniṣṭhās tathaiva ca /
[61.20] taponiṣṭhāś ca boddhavyāḥ karmaniṣṭhāś ca bhārata // [mbh 13.9.43]

[61.21] kavyāni jñānaniṣṭhebhyaḥ pratiṣṭhāpyāni bhārata /
[61.22] tatra ye brāhmaṇān ke cin na ca nindanti te varāḥ* //{531}* [mbh 13.9.44]

[61.23] ye tu nindanti jalpeṣu na tāñ śrāddheṣu bhojayet /
[61.24] brāhmaṇā ninditā rājan hanyus tripuruṣaṃ kulam* //{532}* [mbh 13.9.45]

!{516}! dhn[t] 254 statt dhn[d] 61.2-3: (iti) bhagavaddarśanādiṣu yogyatārahitānāṃ nikṛṣṭānāṃ utkṛṣṭatvādikaṃ na sambhavati. bhagavadarcakānām autkṛṣṭyaṃ.                 

[62.1] vaikhānasānāṃ vacanam ṛṣīṇāṃ śrūyate nṛpa /
[62.2] dūrād eva parīkṣeta brāhmaṇān vedapāragān /
[62.3] priyo vā yadi vā dveṣyaḥ teṣu tac chrāddham āvapet* //{533}* [mbh 13.9.46]

[62.4] yaḥ sahasraṃ sahasrāṇāṃ bhojayed anṛcāṃ naraḥ /
[62.5] ekas tān mantravit pūtaḥ sarvān arhati bhārata* //{534}*" [mbh 13.9.47]

 [aṣṭākṣarādimantrajapaniṣṭhānāṃ mahimā]

[62.6-7] evaṃ aṣṭākṣara dvādaśākṣara puruṣasūktādimantrajapaniṣṭhānāṃ darśanena brahmahā 'pi śuddhyatīti purāṇoktam. yathā*{535}*:
[62.8] *{536}*padmapurāṇe: "sāṅgaṃ samantraṃ sanyāsaṃ sarṣicchandodhidaivatam /
[62.9] sadīkṣāvidhi sadhyānaṃ sayantraṃ dvādaśākṣaram // [padma.p ]

[62.10] sāṣṭākṣarañ ca mantreśaṃ ye japanti narottamāḥ /
[62.11] tān dṛṣṭvā brahmahā śuddhyet kiṃ punar vaiṣṇavas svayam //" iti [padmap ]
[62.12-14] śruyate 'pi. "yo ha vai nārāyaṇasyāṣṭākṣaraṃ padam adhyeti anupabravas sarvam āyur eti vindate prājāpatyaṃ rāyaspoṣaṃ gaupatyaṃ tato 'mṛtatvam aśnute tato 'mṛtatvam aśnuta iti".
[62.15] śrīpāñcarātre kapiñjalasaṃhitāyām:
[62.16] "yājanādhyāpanayutaḥ śiṣyānugrahakārakaḥ /
[62.17] ācārya iti vijñeyo mantratantraparāyaṇaḥ* //{537}* [kapiñjalas]
[62.18] āśrame vā vane vā 'pi sa vaikhānasa ucyate* /{538}*[62.19] grāmyadharmāṇi sarvāṇi varjayed vanavāsakaḥ //"*{539}* iti. [kapiñjalas]
[62.20] yamasmṛtau: "yo 'nucānaṃ*{540}* dvijaṃ martyo hatavān arthalobhataḥ /
[62.21] sa vadet pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ jalasthaś cintayed dharim* //{541}*"
[62.22-24] iti kevalāṣṭākṣaramantrajapaniṣṭhānām apy evaṃ vidhāḥ prabhāvāḥ śrūyanta iti cet śrutismṛtivihitais tair eva mantraiḥ advārakabhagavadarcane mukhyādikāriṇāṃ vaikhānasānāṃ kaimutikanyāyasiddham autkṛṣṭyaṃ kenāpodituṃ śakyam.*{542}*
!{533}! mbh: priyān vā yadi vā dveṣyāṃs.          

 [devalakanirūpaṇam]
[63.1-3] kiñca - yathā vaikhānasānām utpattyādikaṃ śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu viśeṣeṇa pratipāditaṃ tathā itareṣāṃ viśeṣeṇa pratipāditañ cet tadā vaikhānasasāmyam itareṣāṃ syāt. tathā na dṛśyate hi.
[63.4] atha vastuto devalakā nirūpyante.*{543}*
[63.5] vaikhānase: "avaikhānasavipro yaḥ pūjayed ālaye harim /
[63.6] sa vai devalako nāma havyakavyabahiṣkṛtaḥ* //{544}*
[63.7] vaikhānasakule jātaḥ pāñcarātreṇa dīkṣitaḥ /[63.8] na dīkṣito na sañjāto (?) lobhān mohān madarcanam* /{545}*[63.9] kuryāc cet tu viśeṣeṇa bhaved devalakas to saḥ //"*{546}*
 [devalakatraividyam]

[63.10] pāñcarātre saṃkarṣaṇasaṃhitāyām: "karmadevalakāḥ kecit kalpadevalakāḥ pare /
[63.11] śuddhadevalakāś cānye tridhā devalakāḥ smṛtāḥ // [saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]

 [karmadevalakalakṣaṇam]

[63.12] arthārthī kālanirdeśī yo devaṃ pūjayet sa hi /
[63.13] karmadevalako nāma sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ // [saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]

[63.14] pāñcarātravidhānajño dīkṣāvirahito 'rcakaḥ /
[63.15] caturvedādhikāro 'pi kalpadevalakaḥ smṛtaḥ // [saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]

[63.16] āgamoktavidhānajño bhadrakālyupajīvakaḥ*{547}* /
[63.17] śuddhadevalakaḥ proktaḥ sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ // [saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]

[63.18] ārṣoktena vidhānena devalatvaṃ na vidyate /
[63.19] tasmāt sarvaprayatnena vaidikenaiva pūjayet //" iti [saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā]

[63.20] śivaśekharatantre - rudraḥ:
[63.21] "atha devalakān vakṣye śṛṇu devi samāhitā /
[63.22] karmadevalakāḥ kecit kalpadevalakāḥ pare // [śivaśekharatantra]

[63.23] śuddhadevalakās tv anye tridhā devalakāsmṛtāḥ /
[63.24] anyasūtroktamārgeṇa yas saṃvatsarapūjakaḥ //

!{543}! dhn[t] 263-4 statt dhn[d] 63.1-4: punar devalakatvādivicāraḥ. kiñca - yathā vaikhānasānām utpattyādikaṃ śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu viśeṣeṇa pratipāditaṃ evam itareṣāṃ brāhmaṇasāmānyatvena vinā viśeṣeṇa pratipāditaṃ cet tadānīmetādṛguṇaviśiṣṭā vayam iti. tair vaktum ucitam anyathā asaṃtaṃ? nindyām ātmastutiṃ mūḍhetarāḥ svaparagataviśeṣajñāḥ ke vā brūyaḥ? devalakalakṣaṇaṃ nirūpyate yathā.     

 [śivaśekharatantra]

 [kalpadevalakalakṣaṇam]

[64.1] adīkṣitaḥ svayaṃ tantre karmadevalakas tu saḥ /
[64.2] anenaiva prakāreṇa vatsaratryapūjakaḥ /
[64.3] kalpadevalakaḥ proktaḥ sa vai śailasute dhruvam // [śivaśekharatantra]

 [śuddhadevalakalakṣaṇam]

[64.4] ananujñātam ācāryāt āgamaṃ śuśruve ca yaḥ /
[64.5] śīlataḥ tasya śiṣyaś ca śuddhadevalakāv ubhau // [śivaśekharatantra]

 [trividhasyāpi devalakatvasya rudrādiviṣayakatā]

[64.6] tridhā devalakatvaṃ tu na viṣṇuviṣaye kvacit /
[64.7] rudrakālyādiviṣayam etad āgamasaṃmatam //" iti [śivaśekharatantra]

[64.8] smṛtyantare: "śarvaṃ sūryaṃ tathā candraṃ durgādī rudradevatāḥ /
[64.9] yo 'rcayet paṇapūrvaṃ saḥ sadyaḥ patati mānavaḥ //

[64.10] durgā ca bhadrakālī ca buddhaś ca kṣetrapālakaḥ /
[64.11] pañcapūjā ca ity ete pañcadevalakāḥ smṛtāḥ //

[64.12] ādityam ambikāṃ viṣṇuṃ gaṇanāthaṃ maheśvaram /
[64.13] gṛhe pūjā ca ity ete pañcadevalakāḥ smṛtāḥ (?) //" iti*{548}*

[64.14] *{549}*viṣṇudharmottare: "caṇḍikāyāś ca durgāyā jyeṣṭāyā bhairavasya ca /
[64.15] rudrasya pūjakā ye vai te vai devalakāḥ smṛtāḥ //" iti [viṣṇudharmottarap ]

[64.16] viṣṇu: "devārcanaparo yo 'pi*{550}* parārthaṃ vittakāṅkṣayā /
[64.17] caturvedadharo vipraḥ sa caṇḍālasamo bhaved* //{551}*" iti [viṣṇup ]

[64.18-19] *{552}*evam ebhir vacanaiḥ śāstrānanumatamārgeṇa pūjakānāṃ devatāntarapūjakānām eva ca devalakatvaṃ siddhyatīti sphuṭam avagamyate.
[64.20] kiñca: "vṛṣo dharmas samākhyataḥ tasya yaḥ kurute layam /
[64.21] vṛṣalaṃ taṃ vidur devā nikṛṣṭaṃ śvapacād api //"

!{548}! dhn[t] 275 ins. iti kiñca hārīta: vaikhānasās ti ye viprā haripūjanatatparāḥ. na te devalakā proktā viṣṇupādābjasaṃśrayāḥ iti. smṛtiratnākare atri: vaidikenaiva vidhinā daṃbhalobhavivarjitaḥ pūjayed bhaktito viṣṇuṃ sa hi devalako na vai iti. zitiert als "hārīta" in dhn[d] 65.3-4 und als "smṛtyarthasāra" in dhn[d] 65.5-6.     

 [devalakaśabdanirvacanam]

[64.22-65.2] iti vṛṣalaśabdo yathā vedaśāstroktamārgalayakārake vyutpāditaḥ, tathā devalakśabdo 'pi "div krīḍāvijigīṣāvyavahāradyutistutimodamadasvapnakāntigatiṣv" iti dhātvarthānusāreṇa gatyaparaparyāyamārgārthakadivdhātughaṭitassan vedoktamārgalayaprāpake vyutpādayituṃ śakyate iti tatpratīpeṣu vedamārgapratiṣṭhāpakeṣu vaikhānaseṣu na sarvātmanā pravartate. tathā ca:
[65.3] hārītaḥ: "vaikhānasās tu ye viprā haripūjanatatparāḥ /
[65.4] na te devalakāḥ proktā viṣṇupādābjasaṃśrayāt* //{553}*" iti [vṛddhahārīta 8.78]

 [vaikhānasānaṃ devalakaśabdavācyatvābhāvaḥ]

[65.5] smṛtyarthasāre: atri: "vaidikenaiva vidhinā dambhalobhavivarjitaḥ /
[65.6] pūjayed bhaktito viṣṇuṃ sa hi devalako na vai* //{554}*" iti
[65.7-8] *{555}*anyathā śrutyuktamārgeṇālayārcakānām api devalakatve tādṛśālayārcanapratipādakānāṃ śrutismṛtipurāṇādivacanānāṃ vyarthatā syāt.
[65.9-10] *{556}*nanu - ajñānataḥ kṛtam api bhagavadārādhanam apavargapradañ cet. vinā śāstraṃ anadhikāriṇāpi kṛtaṃ tatapavargapradaṃ kiṃ na syād iti cet. na. bhagavadājñābhaṅgāpatteḥ.
[65.11] yathoktaṃ bhagavatā: "yaś śāstravidhim utsṛjya vartate kāmakārataḥ /
[65.12] na sa siddhim avāpnoti na sukhaṃ na parāṃ gatim //" iti [mbh 6.38.23]

[65.13] "śrutismṛtī mamaivājñā yas tām ullaṅghya vartate /
[65.14] ājñācchedī mama drohī madbhakto 'pi na vaiṣṇavaḥ* //{557}*" iti

[65.15] "mama cāpi priyaṃ viṣṇor devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ /
[65.16] mānuṣo vaidikācāraṃ manasā 'pi na laṅghayet //" iti

[65.17-18] *{558}*ataḥ anadhikāriṇā kṛtaṃ śāstrāsammatam iti tantroktaprakāreṇa kṛtam api tat nāpavargapradam.*{559}*
[65.19] nanu: "brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiś ca kṛtalakṣaṇaiḥ /
[65.20] arcanīyaś ca sevyaś ca pūjanīyaś ca mādhavaḥ /
[65.21] sāttvataṃ vidhim āsthāya gītaḥ saṅgarṣaṇena*{560}* yaḥ //"

 [tantrānusāripūjāyāḥ apavargapradatvābhāvaḥ]
[65.22-24] *{561}*iti śūdrādīnām api pāñcarātroktamārgeṇārcane adhikāre siddhe kathaṃ tāntrikoktaprakāreṇārcanaṃ kurvataḥ brāhmaṇādeḥ (anadhikāriṇaḥ) tat apavargapradaṃ na bhavatīty ucyata iti ced ucyate.
!{553}! vṛddhahārīta: na te devalakāḥ jñeyā haripādābjasaṃśrayāt.         

 [caturvidhatantreṣu ekatra dīkṣitasya tantrāntare 'nadhikāraḥ]
[66.1] "prathamaṃ mantrasiddhāntaṃ dvitīyañ cāgamāhvayam / [pādmas caryāpāda 19.112cd][66.2] tṛtīyaṃ tantrasiddhāntaṃ tantrāntaramataḥ param* //{562}*" [pādmas caryāpāda 19.113ab][66.3] iti caturvidheṣu siddhānteṣu[66.4] "ekatra dīkṣitas tantre siddhānte vā dvijottama* /{563}*[66.5] kriyāṃ na kuryād anyatra karṣaṇādi caturmukha // [pādma.s caryāpāda 19.131]
[66.6] ācāryakam athārtvijyaṃ pūjāñ ca madhuvidviṣaḥ /
[66.7] mantre deve ca siddhānte tad evāsya hi yujyate* //{564}*" [pādmas caryāpāda 19.132]
[66.8] iti caturvidhatantreṣu ekatra dīkṣitasya tantrāntare praveśayogyatābhāvasya pratipādanāt*{565}*.[66.9] "ekagotrasamutpannaṃ pañcagotraṃ pṛthak pṛthak / ity ārabhya[66.10] sūtraṃ kātyāyanaṃ śākhāṃ yājuṣaṃ*{566}* śuklam eva ca //
[66.11] aupagāyanaśāṇḍilyau bhāradvājo 'tha gautamaḥ /
[66.12] mauñjāyanis tu pañcaite pāñcarātrādhikāriṇaḥ* //{567}*"
[66.13] ity adhikāribhedasya vidhīyamānatvāt.
 [āpastambādisūtrasaṃskṛtasya pāñcarātroktasaṃskārayogyatābhāvaḥ]

[66.14] "caturṇām api varṇānām itareṣāñ ca tadbhuvām /
[66.15] dīkṣā samaiva sarveṣām ācāras tantravartmanā //" [pādmas caryāpāda 21.55]

 [tantroktaprakāreṇa dīkṣitānām eva tantroktārcanāyām adhikāraḥ]
[66.16-18] ityāpastambādisūtraiḥ*{568}* saṃskṛtasya pāñcarātroktamārgeṇa niṣekādisaṃskārayogyatābhavakathanāt.*{569}* tāntrikoktaprakāreṇa dīkṣitānām eva tantroktārcanāyām adhikāritva sambhavāt.
 [paradharmānuṣṭhātuḥ patitatvādi]

[66.19] "svasūtre vartamāne tu parasūtreṇa vartate /
[66.20] apramāṇam ṛṣiṃ kṛtvā so 'ndhe tamasi majjati //"
[66.21] "svakīyadharmam utsṛjya paradharmaṃ ya āśrayet* /{570}*[66.22] patitas sa bhaved āśu sadya eva na saṃśayaḥ //"
[66.23] "svasūtrasya parityāgāt parasūtrasamāśrayāt /
[66.24] sadyaḥ patati vai vipro na vedasya samāśraye //"*{571}*

!{562}! pādmas: turyaṃ tantrāntaraṃ bhavet.          

[67.1] "śākhāṃ śikhāṃ tathā puṇḍraṃ samayācāram eva ca /
[67.2] pūrvair ācaritaṃ kuryād anyathā patito bhavet //"

[67.3] "yas svaśākhāṃ parityajya paraśākhāsu vartate /
[67.4] śākhāraṇḍas sa vijñeyas sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ* //{572}*" [ās 4.59]

[67.5] "yas svadharmaṃ parityajya paradharmaṃ niṣevate /
[67.6] pāṣaṇḍinaṃ tam āhur vai nikṛṣṭaṃ śvapacād api //" iti.

[67.7] bhagavān: "śreyān svadharmo viguṇaḥ paradharmāt svanuṣṭhitāt /
[67.8] svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmo bhayāvahaḥ* //{573}*" iti. [mbh 6.25.35]

[67.9] vyāsa: "svadharmaṃ yas samutsṛjya paradharmaṃ samāśrayet /
[67.10] anāpadi sa vidvadbhiḥ patitaḥ parikīrtitaḥ //"
[67.11-12] *{574}*ityādibhiś ca vacanaiḥ paradharmānuṣṭhātuḥ patitatvādismaraṇāc ca anyasūtroktaprakāreṇa tāntrikoktena mārgeṇa vā bāhmaṇādibhir*{575}* api anadhikāribhiḥ bhagavadārādhanaṃ kartuṃ na śakyate.
 [śūdrasya pūjāyām anadhikāraḥ]
[67.13] tarhi "brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ" ityādi *{576}*bhāratavacanasya kā gatir iti cet - ucyate.[67.14] *{577}*mādhavāḥ: mukhyatvena advārakabhagavadyajanādhikāritvena nirūpitaiḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ pūjanīyaḥ.
[67.15-16] *{578}*itaraiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiś cārcanīyaḥ. śūdraiḥ strībhiś ca yathārham ijyas sevyaś ca iti tasya vacanasyārthaḥ.
[67.17] "... śūdraiḥ strībhis tathetaraiḥ /
[67.18] yathārham ijyas sevyaś ca nityaṃ sarveśvaro hariḥ //"
[67.19-22] iti bhāradvājavacanāt "arghyāntam arcanaṃ proktaṃ havirantañ ca pūjanam //" ity arcanapūjanayoḥ bhinnārthakatvapratipādanāt, sarvair ekarītyā pūjane 'bhimate ekapadasyaiva paryāptatvāt itarayoḥ padayor vaiyarthyāpātāc ca. anyathā śūdrasyāpi pūjārcanādiṣv adhikārāṅgīkāre śrutismṛtisūtrapurāṇādivirodho bhavet.[67.23-25] śūdrasyānadhikārapratipādakāni vacanāni caitāni. śruti "tasmāc chūdro yajñe 'navakḷptaḥ. sa hi devatā anvasṛjata tasmāc chūdro bahupaśur ayajñīyo daiva" iti.
!{572}! ās: svaśākhāṃ samparityajya paraśākhānusārataḥ / śākhāraṇḍas sa vijñeyas sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ //.       

[68.1] smṛti: "japas tapas tīrthasevā pravrajyā mantrasādhanam /
[68.2] devatārādhanañ caiva strīśūdrapatitāni ṣaṭ //" iti

 [śūdrasyadvijaśuśrūṣaiva dharmaḥ]

[68.3] śrībhāgavate:*{579}* "śuśrūṣaṇaṃ dvijagavāṃ devānāñ cāpy amāyayā /

[68.5] manau: "brāhmaṇasya tapo jñānaṃ tapaḥ kṣatrasya rakṣaṇam /
[68.6] vaiśyasya tu tapo vārtā tapaś śūdrasya sevanam //" iti [manudhś 11.235]

[68.7] anyatra*{581}*: "yadi śūdras tapaḥ kuryād vedadṛṣṭena vartmanā /
[68.8] iha cāsya parikleśaḥ pretya cāsyāśubhā gatiḥ //" iti.
[68.9-11] kimarthaṃ śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣā sarvadā abhihiteti cet - ucyate. janmāntarīyakarmavaśāt jananakāle 'pi tamoguṇair abhibhūtasya tasya śūdrasya tamonirasanārthaṃ dvijaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ brahmaṇā prayuktam.*{582}*[68.12] āśvamedhike: "udite savitar yasya kriyāyuktasya dhīmataḥ / [mbh 14, app. 4.1690][68.13] caturvedadharasyāpi dehe ṣaḍvṛṣalāḥ sthitāḥ* //{583}* [mbh 14, app. 4.1691][68.14] kṣatriye sapta vijñeyā vaiśye tv aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ* /{584}* [mbh 14, app. 4.1692][68.15] niyatāḥ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha śūdre 'ṣṭāviṃśatiḥ khalu* //{585}*" ity ārabhya [mbh 14, app. 4.1693][68.16] "rāgadveṣau ca mohaś ca pāruṣyañ ca nṛśaṃsatā* /{586}* [mbh 14, app. 4.3340][68.17] śāṭhyañ ca dīrghavairañ ca atimānamanārjavam* //{587}* [mbh 14, app. 4.3341][68.18] anṛtañ cāpavādaś ca paiśunyam atilobhatā* /{588}* [mbh 14, app. 4.3342][68.19] hiṃsā steyaṃ mṛṣāvādo vañcanā roṣalobhate* //{589}* [mbh 14, app. 4.3343][68.20] abuddhatā ca nāstikyaṃ bhayam ālasyam eva ca* /{590}* [mbh 14, app. 4.3344][68.21] aśaucañ cākṛtajñatvaṃ dambhatā stambha eva ca* //{591}* [mbh 14, app. 4.3345][68.22] niṣkṛteś cāpy avijñānaṃ janane śūdram āviśan* /{592}* [mbh 14, app. 4.3346][68.23] dṛṣṭvā pitāmahaḥ śūdram abhibhūtan tu tāmasaiḥ // [mbh 14, app. 4.3347][68.24] dvijaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ dharmaṃ śūdrāṇān tu prayuktavān / [mbh 14, app. 4.3348][68.25] naśyanti tāmasā bhāvāḥ śūdrasya dvijabhaktitaḥ //" iti. [mbh 14, app. 4.3349]

 [vaikhānasetarasūtriṇāṃ bhagavadārādhanaprakāraḥ]
[69.1] ataḥ tamoguṇābhibhūtasya śūdrasya bhagavadyajanādhikāro nāsty eva.*{593}*[69.2-7] nanv eṣāṃ*{594}* śaunakādyuktaprakāreṇa bhagavadārādhane 'dhikāro bhaved iti cet*{595}* - tad asat. tatra adhikāriviśeṣapratipādanābhavāt; sāmānyenoktatve 'pi śrutismṛtisūtrapurāṇamahābhāratavaikhānasapāñcarātraśaivaśilpajyautiṣādiṣu adhikāriṇāṃ viśiṣya pratipāditatvāt*{596}* sarvaśākhāpratyayanyāyena sāmānyaviśeṣanyāyena "matprakaraṇādhītaṃ sarvaṃ madartham" iti nyāyena prakaraṇasāmyena*{597}*, upāsya devataikyāt guṇopasaṃhāranyāyena ca śaunakādibhir uktārcanāvidher api atraiva paryavasānaṃ yuktam.

[69.11] tasya tāvati śāstrārthe kṛte sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavet //" iti

[72.4] yatsūryād vaiṣṇavaṃ tejaś śātitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā // [viṣṇu.p ]
[72.5] jājjvalyamānam apatat tadbhūmau munisattama //"iti [viṣṇup ][72.6] evaṃ ca sūryasāvarṇikamanvantaramārabhya ravimaṇḍalasya vṛttākārapratītiḥ.[72.7-8] tad anusāreṇa bodhāyanādibhiḥ vṛttākāratvaṃ ravimamaṇḍalasyoktam. tataḥ pūrvaṃ caturaśratvam va. tad evāsmin sūtre pratipāditam.[72.9-10] evaṃ "vānaprastho vaikhānaśāstrasamudācāro vaikhānasa"*{609}* iti vaikhānasasūtram anusmṛtya tṛtīyāśramadharmān bodhāyanaḥ pratipādayati. [baudhdhs 2.6.11.14][72.11-17] tathā āgnivaiśyasūtre "athātas sūtragaṇanāṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. bodhāyanam āpastambaṃ satyāṣāṭhaṃ drāhyāyaṇam āgastyaṃ śākalyam āśvalāyanaṃ śāmbhavīyaṃ kātyāyanam iti navāni pūrvasūtrāṇi. vaikhānasaṃ śaunakīyaṃ bhāradvājam āgnivaiśyaṃ jaiminīyaṃ *{610}* vādhūlaṃ mādhyandinaṃ hiraṇyakeśīyaṃ kauṣītakam iti navāny aparasūtrāṇi. evam aṣṭādaśasūtrāṇy aṣṭādaśasūtrakārāś ca. etāni caturvedamūlāni. pūrvasūtrāṇi śārīrāṇi sāmānyāni bhavanti. uttarasūtrāṇi vaikhānasādīni viṣṇusaṃbandhīni daivikānī" ti vaikhānasasūtrasyāditvaṃ vaiṣṇavatvañ cocyate.[72.18-19] asya sūtrasyādhikyaṃ ca "ye vaikhānasasūtreṇa saṃskṛtās dvijātaya"*{611}* ityādinā pūrvam eva pratipāditam.[72.20-21] ataḥ sarvasūtrāṇām ādir idaṃ sūtram iti siddham. tataḥ sarvasūtrottamatvañ cāsyopapadyate iti nirūpito dvitīyo hetuḥ.[72.22] iti dvitīyahetunitūpaṇam.
!{609}! baudhdhs: vānaprastho vaikhānasaśāstrasamudācāraḥ.   

 [tṛtīyahetunirūpaṇam]

 [vaikhānasasūtrasya śrutimārgānusāritvam]
[73.1-3] athāsya śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya sūtrāntarāpekṣayā vailakṣaṇyāpādakaṃ pratyakṣaśrutimūlakatvam astīti jñāpayituṃ "sarvakarmasu śrutimārgānusāritvād" iti tṛtīyo hetur nirūpyate. tathā hi:
 [śuddhācamanavidheḥ śrautatvam]
[73.4-9] śuddhācamanavidhau "yattrir ācāmati tena ṛcaḥ prīṇāti" ityādi śrutyanusāreṇa sūtre "ṛgvedaḥ prīṇātv" ityādinā śuddhācamanam uktam. nanu bodhāyanenāpi śuddhācamanavidhir ukta iti cet satyam. "ācamanavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ" ity ārabhya "gokarṇabaddhahastena trir ācamet, prathamaṃ yat pibati tena ṛgvedaṃ prīṇāti yad dvitīyaṃ tena yajurvedaṃ yat tṛtīyaṃ tena sāmavedaṃ prīṇātī"ty ācamanena ṛgvedādīnāṃ prītir bhavatīty uktam. na tu mantraḥ.[73.10-11] śrutismṛtisūtravihitasya sandhyopāsanasya pradhānabhūtam arghyapradānādikam atraiva pratipāditam. "prātas sūryaś cetyādinācamya āpo hiṣṭhādibhis tisṛbhiḥ prokṣya[73.12] gāyatryā 'po 'bhimantrya ādityābhimukhaṃ vikṣipya pradakṣiṇaṃ karoti" ityādi.
[73.13-17] bodhāyanenāpi sandhyāvandanavidhir uktaḥ iti cet naivam. "athātas sandhyopāsanavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. tīraṃ gatvāprayato 'bhiṣiktaḥ prayato vā nābhiṣiktaḥ*{612}* prakṣālipādapāṇir*{613}* apa ācamya surabhimatyā abliṅgābhir vāruṇībhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇābhiḥ pāvamānībhiḥ vyāhṛtibhir anyaiś ca pavitrair ātmānaṃ prokṣya prayato bhavati. athāpy udāharanti." [baudhdhs 2.4.7.1-3]
[73.18] "āpo 'vagāhanaṃ snānaṃ vihitaṃ sārvavarṇikam /
[73.19] mantravatprokṣaṇañ caiva dvijānām avaśiṣyate* //{614}*" iti [baudhdhs 2.4.7.3-2]
[73.20-74.3] sarvakarmaṇāñ caivārambheṣu prāksandhyopāsanākālāc caitenaiva pavitrasamūhenātmānaṃ prokṣya prayato bhavati. athāpy udāharanti. "darbheṣv āsīno darbhān dhārayamāṇaḥ sodakapāṇinā*{615}* pratyaṅmukhaḥ sāvitrīṃ sahasrakṛtvaḥ āvartayet. prāṇāyāmaśo vā śatakṛtvaḥ. tribhiś ca prāṇāyāmaiḥ tato (tānto) brahmahṛdayena. vāruṇībhyāṃ rātrim upatiṣṭhate." ityādinā mārjanādikam uktam. pradhānabhūtam arghyapradānādikam anuktam. [baudhdhs 2.4.7.4-9]
!{612}! baudhdhs: vānabhiṣiktaḥ.    

 [śrutyukto brahmayajñaprakāraḥ]

 [brahmavaraṇapūrvakasomavaraṇam]
[74.4-9] brahmayajñaḥ. talavakāropaniṣadi "tasyā vā eṣa prathamaḥ pādaḥ oṃ bhūs tatsavitur vareṇyaṃ oṃ bhuvaḥ bhargo devasya dhīmahi oṃ suvaḥ dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt iti pacchaḥ, oṃ bhūr bhuvas tatsavitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi oṃ suvaḥ dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt ity ardhacaśaḥ, oṃ bhūrbhuvassuvas tatsavitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt iti samastāñ ca sāvitrīṃ japtveti yathodiṣṭaḥ, tathātra sūtre 'pi ukto 'sti.[74.10-11] āghārādiṣu sarvam api śrautavat. atra brahmavaraṇānantaraṃ somavaraṇam apy uktam asti. "somo 'smākaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ rājā - somarājāno brāhmaṇā" iti.[74.12-13] "viṣṇuś ca vai somaś ca brahmav ādyam avadetāṃ 'ahaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhe'ti viṣṇur abravīt 'ahaṃ pratiṣṭhe'ti somaḥ. tau prajāpatiṃ praśnam aitāṃ so 'bravīt prajāpatiḥ[74.14] 'chandāṃsi viṣṇum adhigacchanti, nakṣatrāṇi somaṃ. tāv ubhau brahmaṇyāv'; iti so 'bravīt.[74.15-17] pūjitau pūjayantau stutau stunvantau priyau priyavantau brahmaṇyau brahmavittau brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhātārau bhavata iti yan māṃ brahmaṇā vakṣyanti yajñeṣu so 'ham iti viṣṇur abravīt. tasmād viṣṇur yajño brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhā iti. vijñayate ca.[74.18-22] "brāhmaṇo vai chandāṃsī"ty etasmāt brāhmaṇāt yan māṃ brāhmaṇā vakṣyanti nakṣatreṣu tatrāham iti so 'bravīt. tasmāt brāhmaṇānāṃ somo rājeti tasmād vijñāyate ca brāhmaṇe vā aṣṭāviṃśo nakṣatrāṇāṃ tasya vacaḥ puṇyam iti tāv ubhau brahmaṇyau brahmavittau brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhātārau brāhmaṇeṣu pratiṣṭhitau ya evaṃ brāhmaṇapuraskṛtāni karmāṇi karoti yajñasya samṛddhyā" iti ca śrutiprasiddhatvāt.[74.23-25] evam atra śāntikapauṣṭikādiṣu pradhānakarmatvāt navagrahamakhasya pañcāgnikuṇḍavidhānam uktam. "atha grahaśāntiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. grahyāyattā lokayātrā tasmād ātmaviruddhe prāpte grahān samyak pūjayatī" ti.
 [grahaśānteḥ prādhānyam]
[75.1-8] grahaśānteḥ kathaṃ prādhānyam iti ced ucyate. "udyantam astaṃyantam ādityam abhidhyāyan kurvan brāhmaṇo vidvān sakalaṃ bhadram aśnute 'sāv ādityo brahmeti brahmaiva san brahmāpy eti ya evaṃ veda" iti "ya eṣo 'ntarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣo dṛśyate" iti "yo 'sau tapann udeti" ityādi "viṣṇuśakter avasthānaṃ sadāditye karoti ca" iti "dhyeyas sadā savitṛmaṇḍalamadhyavartī" tyādibhiś ca vacanaiḥ yat pratipāditaṃ savitṛmaṇḍalamadhyavartino bhagavato nārāyaṇasya yajanaṃ tad evedam ity abhiprāyeṇa sūtrakārair asya grahayajñasya prādhānyam uktam. tathānte "anyathā mahattaro doṣo bhavatī"ty apy uktam.[75.9] bodhāyanaś ca: "athāto grahātithyabalikarmopahārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ"
 [savitṛhomaḥ]

[75.10] aśraddhadhānam aśucim ajapaṃ tyaktamaṅgalam /
[75.11] grahā nayanti suvyaktaṃ puruṣaṃ yamasādanam //

[75.12] grahāṇām ugraceṣṭānāṃ nakṣatrapathacāriṇām /
[75.13] upahārān pravakṣyāmi śāntyarthan tu yathāvidhi //"

 [viṣṇvārādhanasya śrautatvam]

[75.14-16] māsi māsy ṛtāv ṛtau candragrahe sūryagrahe viṣuve 'yane śubhāśubhe janmanakṣatre tadgrahāṇām ātithyaṃ saṃvatsarād api prayuñjānaḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnoti" iti grahaśāntikālaṃ nirūpya.
[75.17] "grahā gāvo narendrāś ca brāhmaṇāś ca viśeṣataḥ /
[75.18] pūjitāḥ pūjayanty enaṃ nirdahanty avamānitāḥ //"
[75.19] ity akaraṇe pratyavāyam api darśitavān.[75.20-22] tasmād eva sūtrakāraiḥ sūryacandrau vinā lokapravṛtty asambhavāt sūryapradhānatvāc ca grahāṇāṃ sarvakarmaṇām ādau grahapuraskāram uktvā tatra pañcāgnikuṇḍavidhānam upadiśya pradhāne sabhye viṣṇurūpasya savituḥ homaḥ "sabhye savitur" iti pratipāditaḥ.[75.23-24] evam - "nārāyaṇa paraṃ brahma" - "brahmaiva bhūtānāṃ jyeṣṭhāṃ tena ko 'rhati spardhitum" - "agnir vai devānām avamo viṣṇuḥ paramaḥ tadantareṇa sarvā anyā devatāḥ"
 [śrutimūlakatve prāmāṇyātiśayaḥ]
[76.1] ityādi śrutyanusāreṇa "tasmād gṛhe paramaṃ viṣṇuṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sāyaṃprātarhomānte 'rcayati"[76.2-3] iti nārāyaṇaparatvena sūtrāntareṣv anuktam ārādhanavidhim uktvā tatra "sa vā eṣa puruṣaḥ pañcadhā pañcātmā" ityādi śrutyanusāreṇa pañcamūrtividhānam apy uktam.[76.4-5] āghārādiṣu śrautavad eveti pratyakṣasiddham iti pūrvam evoktam. evam anyatrāpi draṣṭavyam.
[76.6-7] śrutimārgānusāritve ko viśeṣa iti cet - ucyate. śrutimūlatve hi prāmāṇyātiśayasambhavaḥ. yathāha
[76.8] manu: "vedaḥ smṛtiḥ sadācāraḥ svasya ca priyam ātmanaḥ /
[76.9] etac catuṣṭayaṃ prāhuḥ*{616}* sākṣād dharmasya lakṣaṇam // [manudhś 2.12]

[76.10] sarvaṃ tu samavekṣyaitad akhilaṃ jñānacakṣuṣā*{617}* /
[76.11] śrutiprāmāṇyato vidvān svadharme niviśeta vai //" [manudhś 2.8]

[76.12] śrībhārate: "vedapraṇihito dharmo hy adharmas tadviparyayaḥ /
[76.13] vedo nārāyaṇas sākṣāt svayambhūr iti śuśrumaḥ //" [mbh ]

[76.14] pracetā: "amīṃāṃsyā bahiśśāstrā ye cānye vedabarjitaḥ /
[76.15] yattadbrūyur na tatkuryād vedād dharmo vidhīyate //"
[76.16] smṛtyantare: "dharmaṃ jijñāsamānānāṃ pramāṇaṃ prathamaṃ śrutiḥ / [mbh 14 app. 4.2492][76.17] dvitīyaṃ dharmaśāstrān tu*{618}* tṛtīyaṃ lokasaṅgrahaḥ* //{619}*" iti [mbh 14 app. 4.2493][76.18-20] etāvatā sarvakarmasu śrutimārgānusāritva rūpaḥ tṛtīyo hetur nirūpito bhavati. tathā ca śrutimārgānusāritvād asya sūtrasya sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ siddhyati iti nirūpitas tṛtīyo hetuḥ.[76.21] iti tṛtīyahetunirūpaṇam.
!{616}! manudhś: etac caturvidhaṃ prāhuḥ.    

 [caturthahetunirūpaṇam]

 [vaikhānasasūtrasya samantrakasarvakriyāpratipādakatvam]
[77.1-2] idānīṃ tāvat vaikhānasasūtroktadharmānuṣṭhānena anantasthiraphalaprāptiḥ satkulīnatvaṃ phalabhūyastvam api bhavatīti jñāpayituṃ "samantrakasarvakriyāpratipādakatvād" iti caturtho hetu nirūpyate. tad yathā:[77.4-10] atra sūtra*{620}* nityānuṣṭhānavidhau "indro 'ham ubhābhyām" ity ārabhya karaprakṣālanādīni samantrakatvenoktāni. brahmayajñe "ṛtañ ca satyañ ce" ty ādi viśeṣaḥ. puṇyāhe samantrakatvaṃ spaṣṭam. sūtrāntareṣv anuktam aupāsanāgnikuṇdavidhānaṃ pratipāditam. āghāravidhau samantrakatvaṃ siddham. antahome tathaiva. nāndīmukhapūrvakopanayanādiṣu śārīreṣu saṃskāreṣu samantrakatvaṃ pratyakṣam. sthālīpākādiṣu "pūrvavad" ity anena pūrvaṃ vistareṇa pratipāditasyāghāravidheḥ prayogasaukaryārthaṃ saṃkṣepeṇa pratipādanam.
 [aparakriyāyām api samantrakatvam]
[77.11-15] aparakriyāyām apy asti samantrakatvam. tatra kvacit "tūṣṇīm" ity uktvatvāt samantrakatvaṃ nāstīti svayam evāśaṅkya prakārāntareṇa samantrakatvaṃ pratyapādayat. tatra tatra kvacit mantrayogyatābhāve 'pi vihitaviśaye sarvatra samantrakatvam astīty avagamyate. sūtrāntareṣu vihitaviśayeṣv api samantrakatvānukteḥ teṣāṃ samantrakasarvakriyātvaṃ nāsti. tatra aparakriyāyām api sūtrāntarānapekṣā dṛśyate.[77.16-19] bodhāyanena agnimukhādiṣu paridhiparistaraṇādikṣepaṇam tūṣṇīm evoktam. samantrakatvena karmaṇām uktau ko viśeṣa iti cet - ucyate. karmaṇāṃ mantravattve hi vīryavattaratvaṃ karmārādhya bhagavatprīṇanadvārā anantasthiraphalaprāptiḥ satkulīnatvañ ca bhavantīti smṛtipurāṇādiṣv avagamyate. yathā
 [karmaṇām samantrakatve vīryavattaratvam]
[77.20-22] chāndogye: "yad eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayopaniṣadā tad eva vīryavattaraṃ bhavatī"ti. tatraivaṃ vyākhyātam. "mantraprakāśitāni karmāṇi kriyante nāmantra kam asti karme"ti.
!{620}! lies: sūtre. 

 [mantrahīnakarmanindā]

[78.1] ātharvaṇe: "ṛgyajussāmākhyā (?) mantreṣu karmāṇi kavayo yāny apaśyann iti"
[78.2] āraṇyaparvaṇi: "vratopanayanābhyāṃ vā upavāsena vā dvijaḥ /
[78.3] kriyāmantraiś ca saṃyukto brāhmaṇas syān na saṃśayaḥ //" [mbh 3.81.134]

[78.4] tatraiva: "guṇābhāve phalaṃ nyūnaṃ bhavaty aphalam eva vā /
[78.5] anārambhe tu na phalaṃ na guṇo dṛśyate hy utaḥ* //{621}*" iti [mbh 3.33.48]

[78.6] bṛhannāradīye: "amantrato havir yat tu hūyate jātavedase /
[78.7] apātre dīyate yac ca tad ghoraṃ bhogasādhanam // [bṛhannāradap.]

[78.8] hutaṃ haviś cāśucinā dattaṃ yatkarma yatkṛtam /
[78.9] tatsarvaṃ tava bhāgārham adhaḥpātaphalaprada //" [bṛhannāradap]

[78.10] iti balicakravartinaṃ prati bhagavatā vāmanenoktam.
[78.11] bodhāyana: "gobhir aśvaiś ca yānaiś ca kṛṣyā rājopasevayā /
[78.12] kulāny akulatāṃ yānti yāni hīnāni mantrataḥ* //{622}* [baudhdhs 1.5.10.28]

[78.13] mantratas susamṛddhāni*{623}* kulāny alpadhanāny api /
[78.14] kulasaṃkhyāṃ ca gacchanti karṣanti ca mahad yaśaḥ* //{624}*" [baudhdhs 1.5.10.29]

[78.15] manur api: "kuvivāhaiḥ kriyālopair vedānadhyayanena ca /
[78.16] kulāny akulatāṃ yānti brāhmaṇātikrameṇa ca // [manudhś 3.63]

[78.17] śilpena vyavahāreṇa śuddhāpatyaiś ca kevalaiḥ*{625}* /
[78.18] gobhir aśvaiś ca yānaiś ca kṛṣyā rājopasevayā* //{626}* [manudhś 3.64]

[78.19] ayājyayājanāc caiva nāstikyena ca karmaṇā*{627}* /
[78.20] kulāny akulatāṃ yānti yāni hīnāni mantrataḥ*{628}* // [manudhś 3.65]
[78.21] mantratas tu samṛddhāni kulāny alpadhanāni ca* /{629}*[78.22] kulasaṃkhyāṃ ca gacchanti karṣanti ca mahad yaśaḥ* //{630}*" [manudhś 3.66]
!{621}! mbh: na guṇo dṛśyate 'cyuta.          

[79.1] mantrapūtan tu yac chrāddham" iti somotpattau smaryate.
[79.2] śrīgītāyāñ ca: "vidhihīnam asṛṣṭānnaṃ mantrahīnam adakṣiṇam /
[79.3] śraddhāvirahitaṃ yajñaṃ tāmasaṃ paricakṣate //" ity uktam. [bhgī = mbh 6.39.13]
[79.4-5] yathopāsanaṃ phalam iti ca śrutisiddhaṃ "yathā kratur asmin loke puruṣo bhavati tathetaḥ pretya bhavatī"ti.[79.6-7] ataḥ śārīreṣu saṃskāreṣu samantrakasarvakriyāpratipādanāt pūrṇatvaṃ, pūrṇatvād eva sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ cāsya sūtrasya siddham iti nirūpitaḥ caturtho hetuḥ.[79.8] iti caturthahetunirūpaṇam.
 [pañcamahetunirūpaṇam; vaikhānasasūtrasya niṣekādisaṃskārapratipādakatvam]
[80.1] atha pañcamahetunirūpaṇam.[80.2-5] athāsya śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya sarvottamatve tatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhātṝṇām api sarvotkṛṣṭatve ca itarasūtriṣu mukhyatvenānupapannaṃ niṣekādisaṃskārādimattvam*{631}* asya sūtrasya mukhyata evopapadyata iti jñāpayituṃ niṣekādisaṃskārādimatvād iti pañcamo hetur nirūpyate. yathā:
 [saṃskāreṣu niṣekasya prathamatvam]
[80.6] "atha niṣekādisaṃskārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ, ṛtusaṅgamane"ty upakramya[80.7] "pāṇigrahaṇānī"*{632}*ty antena śārīrasaṃskārā niṣekasaṃskārapūrvakatvena pratipāditāḥ.
 [niṣekam antareṇa prajotpattyasaṃbhavaḥ]

[80.8-11] nanu: jātakopanayanavivāhānāntarabhāvino*{633}* niṣekasya katham āditvaṃ pratipādyate? tathā "brāhmaṇo 'sya mukham āsīt"*{634}* "manasā tv eva bhūtāni pūrvaṃ dakṣo 'sṛjat tadā" ityādi śrutismṛtiṣu niṣekena vinā utpattidarśanāc ca niṣekasya kim artham āditvaṃ pratipādyate? jātakasyāditvaṃ śrībhārate cāvagamyate.
[80.12] "jātakarmādibhir yais tu*{635}* saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtaś śuciḥ /
[80.13] vedādhyayanasampannaṣ ṣaṭsu karmasv avasthitaḥ // [mb.h 12.182.2]

[80.14] śaucācāraratas samyak bhikṣārthī ca gurupriyaḥ*{636}* /
[80.15] nityavratas*{637}* satyaparaḥ sa vai brāhmaṇa ucyate //" iti [mbh 12.182.3]

[80.16] evaṃ harivaṃśe: *{638}*"kva dārāḥ kva ca saṃsargaḥ*{639}* kva ca bhāvaviparyayaḥ /
[80.17] yadiyaṃ brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā manasā mānasī prajā // [hariv 35.42]

[80.18] yady asti tapaso vīryaṃ yuṣmākaṃ viditātmanāṃ*{640}* /
[80.19] sṛjadhvaṃ mānasān putrān prājāpatyena karmaṇā //" [hariv 35.43]
[80.20] iti niṣekaṃ vināpi utpattiḥ śrūyate iti niṣekasyāditvaṃ na saṃbhavati iti cet -[80.21-23] tad asat. "niṣekavirahe 'pi utpattis saṃbhavatī"ty etan nopapadyate. tapobalād yogabalāc ca bhagavato nārāyaṇasya brahmaṇo maharṣīṇāṃ vā mānasaprajāsṛṣṭau śaktis sambhavati. nānyeṣām. yathā:*{641}*
!{631}! vgl. dhn[d] 2.7: niṣekasaṃskārādimatvāt.           
[81.1] śrīviṣṇupurāṇe: "saṅkalpād darśanāt sparśāt pūrveṣām abhavan prajāḥ" [viṣṇup ][81.2] tapoviṣeśair iddhānāṃ tadātyantatapasvinām* //{642}*" [viṣṇup 1.15.79]
[81.3] "yuge yuge bhavanty ete dakṣādyā munisattamāḥ /
[81.4] punaś caiva niruddhyante vidvāṃs tatra na muhyati // [viṣṇup 1.15.83]
[81.5] kāniṣṭhyaṃ śryaiṣṭhyam apy eṣāṃ pūrvaṃ nāsti dvijottama* //{643}* [viṣṇup 1.15.84ab][81.6] tapa eva garīyo 'bhūt prabhāvaś caiva kāraṇam //" iti [viṣṇup ]
 [niṣekenaiva rudrasyāpi utpattiḥ]
[81.7] rudrotpattir api niṣekeneti śrūyate. śatapathe: "abhūd vā idaṃ sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhā"[81.8-10] ity ārabhya "bhūtānāñ ca prajāpatis saṃvatsarāyādikṣata*{644}* bhūtānāṃ grahapatir āsīd uṣā patnī"*{645}*ty ādikam uktvā "bhūtānāṃ patiḥ saṃvatsara uṣasi reto 'siñcat saṃvatsare kumāro 'jāyata tasya rudrasya nāma karotī"*{646}*ty ādi.
 [niṣekakriyāprakāraḥ]
[81.11-13] niṣekakriyāprakāro 'pi śrūyate hi. "nagnaṃ kṛtvorum upapravartayati yadā hi nagna ūrur bhavaty atha mithunībhavato 'tha retas sicyate 'tha prajāḥ prajāyante" iti, "retasa eva siktasya bahuśo rūpāṇi vikaroti sa vai prajāyate śvaḥ śvo*{647}* bhūyān bhavatī"ti,[81.14-18] "reto mūtraṃ vijahāti yoniṃ praviśad indriyaṃ garbho jarāyuṇā vṛtaḥ ulbaṃ jahāti janmanā"*{648}* iti. muṇḍopaniṣadi - "pumān retas siñcati yoṣitāyāṃ bahvyaḥ*{649}* prajās sṛjamānās sarūpāḥ"*{650}* iti. chāndogye - "yoṣā vā va gautamāgnir" ity ārabhya "tasya upastha eva samid. yad antaḥ karoti te 'rciṣā.*{651}* abhinandā visphuliṅgās. tasminn agnau*{652}* devā reto juhvati. tasyā āhuter garbhas*{653}* sambhavatī"*{654}*ti ca.
 [sṛṣṭikālād ārabhya niṣekād evotpattiḥ]

[81.19] śrīviṣṇupurāṇe: "prajās sṛjeti vyādiṣṭaḥ pūrvaṃ dakṣas svayambhuvā /
[81.20] yathā sasarja bhūtāni tathā śruṇu mahāmate* //{655}* [viṣṇup 1.15.86]

[81.21] manasā tv eva bhūtāni pūrvaṃ dakṣo 'sṛjat tadā /
[81.22] devān ṛṣīṃs tu gandharvān asurān pannagāṃs tathā* //{656}* [viṣṇup 1.15.87]
